## üéØ Complete Quick Reference Guide

### **Essential Formulas**

#### **Recovery Rate Calculation**
```
Recovery Rate = (Recovered Carts / Total Abandoned Carts) √ó 100

Example:
Total Abandoned: 1,000
Recovered: 250
Recovery Rate: (250 / 1,000) √ó 100 = 25%
```

#### **Revenue Recovered**
```
Revenue Recovered = Recovered Carts √ó Average Order Value

Example:
Recovered Carts: 250
AOV: $150
Revenue Recovered: 250 √ó $150 = $37,500
```

#### **ROI Calculation**
```
ROI = ((Net Revenue - Total Costs) / Total Costs) √ó 100

Where:
Net Revenue = Revenue Recovered - Discount Cost
Total Costs = Discount Cost + Platform Cost + Development Cost

Example:
Revenue Recovered: $50,000
Discount Cost: $10,000
Platform Cost: $6,000
Development Cost: $5,000

Net Revenue: $50,000 - $10,000 = $40,000
Total Costs: $10,000 + $6,000 + $5,000 = $21,000
ROI: (($40,000 - $21,000) / $21,000) √ó 100 = 90.5%
```

### **Timing Guidelines**

#### **Standard Sequence**
```
Email 1: 1-2 hours after abandon
Email 2: 24 hours after abandon
Email 3: 48 hours after abandon
Email 4: 72 hours after abandon
```

#### **Fast Track (High-Value)**
```
Email 1: 30 minutes after abandon
Email 2: 6 hours after abandon
Email 3: 24 hours after abandon
Email 4: 48 hours after abandon
```

#### **Slow Track (Low-Value)**
```
Email 1: 2 hours after abandon
Email 2: 48 hours after abandon
Email 3: 7 days after abandon
Email 4: 14 days after abandon
```

### **Discount Guidelines**

#### **By Cart Value**
```
$0-50: 10-12% discount
$50-100: 12-15% discount
$100-200: 15-18% discount
$200-500: 18-22% discount
$500+: 22-30% discount
```

#### **By Customer Segment**
```
New Customer: 15-20% discount
Returning Customer: 18-22% discount
VIP Customer: 22-30% discount
```

### **Performance Benchmarks**

#### **Email Metrics**
```
Open Rate: 25-35% (good), 35%+ (excellent)
Click Rate: 5-10% (good), 10%+ (excellent)
Click-to-Open: 15-25% (good), 25%+ (excellent)
Unsubscribe Rate: <0.5% (good), <0.2% (excellent)
```

#### **Recovery Metrics**
```
Recovery Rate: 15-25% (good), 25%+ (excellent)
Conversion Rate: 10-20% (good), 20%+ (excellent)
Revenue per Email: $5-15 (good), $15+ (excellent)
ROI: 300-500% (good), 500%+ (excellent)
```

## üìã Complete Implementation Checklist

### **Week 1: Foundation Setup**

#### **Day 1-2: Technical Setup**
```
‚ñ° Set up cart tracking
‚ñ° Configure email platform
‚ñ° Set up analytics tracking
‚ñ° Test email delivery
‚ñ° Verify tracking works
```

#### **Day 3-4: Template Creation**
```
‚ñ° Create email template 1 (reminder)
‚ñ° Create email template 2 (value)
‚ñ° Create email template 3 (discount)
‚ñ° Create email template 4 (final)
‚ñ° Test all templates
```

#### **Day 5-7: Initial Sequence**
```
‚ñ° Set up email sequence
‚ñ° Configure timing
‚ñ° Add personalization
‚ñ° Test sequence
‚ñ° Launch to small test group
```

### **Week 2: Optimization**

#### **Day 8-10: Segmentation**
```
‚ñ° Create customer segments
‚ñ° Set up segment-based sequences
‚ñ° Configure dynamic content
‚ñ° Test segmentation
‚ñ° Monitor performance
```

#### **Day 11-14: A/B Testing**
```
‚ñ° Set up A/B test framework
‚ñ° Create test variants
‚ñ° Launch subject line tests
‚ñ° Launch CTA tests
‚ñ° Analyze results
```

### **Week 3-4: Expansion**

#### **Week 3: Multi-Channel**
```
‚ñ° Set up SMS recovery
‚ñ° Configure push notifications
‚ñ° Set up display retargeting
‚ñ° Integrate all channels
‚ñ° Test multi-channel flow
```

#### **Week 4: Advanced Features**
```
‚ñ° Implement advanced personalization
‚ñ° Set up predictive scoring
‚ñ° Create advanced segments
‚ñ° Build analytics dashboards
‚ñ° Document processes
```

## üé® Complete Design Templates

### **HTML Email Template Structure**

#### **Basic Structure**
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Abandoned Cart Recovery</title>
    <style>
        /* Email-safe CSS */
        body {
            margin: 0;
            padding: 0;
            font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
            background-color: #f4f4f4;
        }
        .container {
            max-width: 600px;
            margin: 0 auto;
            background-color: #ffffff;
        }
        .header {
            padding: 20px;
            text-align: center;
            background-color: #ffffff;
        }
        .content {
            padding: 20px;
        }
        .product {
            margin: 20px 0;
            padding: 15px;
            border: 1px solid #e0e0e0;
            border-radius: 5px;
        }
        .cta-button {
            display: inline-block;
            padding: 15px 30px;
            background-color: #007bff;
            color: #ffffff;
            text-decoration: none;
            border-radius: 5px;
            font-weight: bold;
            margin: 20px 0;
        }
        .footer {
            padding: 20px;
            text-align: center;
            font-size: 12px;
            color: #666666;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <div class="header">
            <img src="[LOGO_URL]" alt="[BRAND_NAME]" width="150">
        </div>
        <div class="content">
            <h1>Hi [FIRST_NAME],</h1>
            <p>You left some items in your cart:</p>
            
            <div class="product">
                <img src="[PRODUCT_IMAGE]" alt="[PRODUCT_NAME]" width="100">
                <h3>[PRODUCT_NAME]</h3>
                <p>$[PRICE] x [QUANTITY]</p>
            </div>
            
            <p><strong>Total: $[CART_TOTAL]</strong></p>
            
            <a href="[CART_URL]" class="cta-button">Complete Purchase</a>
            
            <p>Questions? Reply to this email.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="footer">
            <p>[COMPANY_NAME] | [ADDRESS]</p>
            <p><a href="[UNSUBSCRIBE_URL]">Unsubscribe</a></p>
        </div>
    </div>
</body>
</html>
```

### **Responsive Design**

#### **Media Queries**
```css
@media only screen and (max-width: 600px) {
    .container {
        width: 100% !important;
    }
    .cta-button {
        display: block !important;
        width: 100% !important;
        text-align: center !important;
    }
    .product {
        width: 100% !important;
    }
}
```

## üöÄ Complete Automation Recipes

### **Recipe 1: Smart Recovery Sequence**

#### **Zapier/Make.com Workflow**
```
Trigger: Cart Abandoned (Webhook)
    ‚Üì
Action 1: Calculate Customer Score
    ‚Üì
IF Score > 80:
    ‚Üí Send Email 1 (30 minutes)
    ‚Üí Send Email 2 (6 hours)
    ‚Üí Send Email 3 (24 hours)
ELIF Score 50-80:
    ‚Üí Send Email 1 (1 hour)
    ‚Üí Send Email 2 (24 hours)
    ‚Üí Send Email 3 (48 hours)
ELSE:
    ‚Üí Send Email 1 (2 hours)
    ‚Üí Send Email 2 (48 hours)
    ‚Üí Send Email 3 (7 days)
```

### **Recipe 2: Engagement-Based Timing**

#### **Workflow Logic**
```
Email 1 Sent
    ‚Üì
Wait 6 hours
    ‚Üì
Check Engagement
    ‚Üì
IF Opened + Clicked:
    ‚Üí Pause sequence
    ‚Üí Wait 24 hours
    ‚Üí IF no purchase: Send Email 2 (trust building)
ELIF Opened but not clicked:
    ‚Üí Send Email 2 (6h later, different angle)
ELIF Not opened:
    ‚Üí Send Email 2 (24h later, standard)
    ‚Üì
Repeat for Email 3 and 4
```

### **Recipe 3: Multi-Channel Orchestration**

#### **Complete Flow**
```
Cart Abandoned
    ‚Üì
Email 1 (1 hour)
    ‚Üì
Wait 2 hours
    ‚Üì
IF not opened:
    ‚Üí SMS (2 hours)
    ‚Üí Push Notification (2.5 hours)
    ‚Üì
IF not clicked:
    ‚Üí Display Ad (3 hours)
    ‚Üì
Email 2 (24 hours)
    ‚Üì
Wait 2 hours
    ‚Üì
IF not opened:
    ‚Üí SMS (26 hours)
    ‚Üí Push Notification (26.5 hours)
    ‚Üì
IF not clicked:
    ‚Üí Display Ad (27 hours)
    ‚Üì
Email 3 (48 hours)
    ‚Üì
IF high-value + no engagement:
    ‚Üí Phone Call (50 hours)
```

## üìä Complete Analytics Formulas

### **Key Metrics Calculations**

#### **Recovery Rate**
```
Recovery Rate = (Recovered Carts / Total Abandoned Carts) √ó 100

Example:
Total Abandoned: 1,000
Recovered: 250
Recovery Rate: 25%
```

#### **Revenue per Email**
```
Revenue per Email = Total Revenue Recovered / Total Emails Sent

Example:
Revenue Recovered: $50,000
Emails Sent: 4,000
Revenue per Email: $12.50
```

#### **Discount Efficiency**
```
Discount Efficiency = Revenue Recovered / Discount Cost

Example:
Revenue Recovered: $50,000
Discount Cost: $10,000
Discount Efficiency: 5.0x
```

#### **Customer Lifetime Value Impact**
```
CLV Impact = (Recovered Customers √ó Average CLV) - Recovery Costs

Example:
Recovered Customers: 250
Average CLV: $500
Recovery Costs: $21,000

CLV Impact: (250 √ó $500) - $21,000 = $104,000
```

### **Predictive Metrics**

#### **Recovery Probability Score**
```
Score = (Cart Value √ó 0.3) + 
        (Customer Segment √ó 0.25) + 
        (Time Since Abandon √ó 0.2) + 
        (Engagement Level √ó 0.15) + 
        (Product Category √ó 0.1)

Where:
- Cart Value: 0-100 (normalized)
- Customer Segment: 0-100 (VIP=100, New=50)
- Time Since Abandon: 0-100 (recent=100, old=0)
- Engagement Level: 0-100 (high=100, low=0)
- Product Category: 0-100 (high-value=100)
```

#### **Optimal Discount Calculator**
```
Optimal Discount = Base Discount + 
                   (Cart Value Factor √ó 0.05) + 
                   (Customer Segment Factor √ó 0.03) + 
                   (Time Factor √ó 0.02) + 
                   (Inventory Factor √ó 0.02)

Where:
- Base Discount: 10%
- Cart Value Factor: 0-5% (based on value)
- Customer Segment Factor: 0-3% (VIP=3%, New=0%)
- Time Factor: 0-2% (older=higher)
- Inventory Factor: 0-2% (low stock=higher)
```

## üí° Complete Best Practices Summary

### **Email Content**

#### **Do's**
```
‚úÖ Personalize with first name
‚úÖ Show cart contents clearly
‚úÖ Include product images
‚úÖ Add social proof
‚úÖ Create urgency (when appropriate)
‚úÖ Make CTAs clear and prominent
‚úÖ Include trust elements
‚úÖ Mobile-optimize everything
‚úÖ Test before sending
‚úÖ Monitor performance
```

#### **Don'ts**
```
‚ùå Send too frequently
‚ùå Use generic messaging
‚ùå Overuse urgency
‚ùå Ignore mobile users
‚ùå Forget to test
‚ùå Use spam trigger words
‚ùå Make false promises
‚ùå Complicate the message
‚ùå Ignore analytics
‚ùå Set and forget
```

### **Timing**

#### **Best Practices**
```
‚úÖ Send Email 1 within 1-2 hours
‚úÖ Space emails appropriately
‚úÖ Consider time zones
‚úÖ Avoid weekends (unless B2C)
‚úÖ Test optimal send times
‚úÖ Adjust based on engagement
‚úÖ Don't send too late at night
‚úÖ Don't send too early in morning
```

### **Discounts**

#### **Best Practices**
```
‚úÖ Start without discount (Email 1)
‚úÖ Escalate gradually
‚úÖ Don't over-discount
‚úÖ Test discount levels
‚úÖ Consider non-discount incentives
‚úÖ Track discount efficiency
‚úÖ Segment by customer value
‚úÖ Don't devalue your brand
```

### **Segmentation**

#### **Best Practices**
```
‚úÖ Segment by cart value
‚úÖ Segment by customer type
‚úÖ Segment by engagement
‚úÖ Segment by product category
‚úÖ Use multiple dimensions
‚úÖ Test segmentation strategies
‚úÖ Refine based on results
‚úÖ Don't over-segment
```

## üîß Complete Technical Reference

### **Email Client Support**

#### **HTML Support**
```
‚úÖ Gmail (Web, iOS, Android)
‚úÖ Outlook (2016, 2019, 365)
‚úÖ Apple Mail (macOS, iOS)
‚úÖ Yahoo Mail
‚úÖ AOL Mail
‚úÖ Mobile clients (iOS, Android)
```

#### **CSS Support**
```
Supported:
- Inline styles
- Media queries (limited)
- Basic selectors
- Color values

Not Supported:
- External stylesheets
- Advanced selectors
- CSS animations
- Flexbox/Grid
```

### **Tracking Parameters**

#### **UTM Parameters**
```
Standard:
- utm_source=abandoned_cart
- utm_medium=email
- utm_campaign=cart_recovery
- utm_content=email_[NUMBER]
- utm_term=[SEGMENT]

Example:
?utm_source=abandoned_cart&utm_medium=email&utm_campaign=cart_recovery&utm_content=email_1&utm_term=high_value
```

#### **Custom Parameters**
```
- cart_id=[CART_ID]
- customer_id=[CUSTOMER_ID]
- discount_code=[DISCOUNT_CODE]
- segment=[SEGMENT]
- email_number=[NUMBER]
```

### **API Endpoints**

#### **Cart Tracking**
```
POST /api/cart/track
Body: {
    cart_id: string,
    customer_email: string,
    items: array,
    total: number,
    timestamp: datetime
}
```

#### **Abandonment Detection**
```
POST /api/cart/abandon
Body: {
    cart_id: string,
    customer_email: string,
    abandoned_at: datetime
}
```

#### **Recovery Tracking**
```
POST /api/cart/recover
Body: {
    cart_id: string,
    customer_email: string,
    recovered_at: datetime,
    email_number: number
}
```

## üéØ Complete Strategy Matrix

### **Strategy Selection Guide**

#### **By Business Type**

**E-commerce (Fashion):**
```
Primary Strategy: Value-First + Progressive Discount
Timing: Fast (1h, 6h, 24h, 48h)
Discount: 15-25%
Channels: Email + SMS + Display
Focus: Visual content, style, trends
```

**E-commerce (Electronics):**
```
Primary Strategy: Educational + Trust Building
Timing: Standard (2h, 24h, 48h, 7d)
Discount: 12-20%
Channels: Email + Display
Focus: Specs, reviews, support
```

**E-commerce (Home & Garden):**
```
Primary Strategy: Lifestyle + Seasonal
Timing: Standard (3h, 48h, 7d, 14d)
Discount: 15-22%
Channels: Email + Display
Focus: Inspiration, decor, seasonal
```

**SaaS/Software:**
```
Primary Strategy: Value-First + Trial Extension
Timing: Fast (1h, 6h, 24h, 48h)
Discount: 20-30% (annual plans)
Channels: Email + In-app
Focus: Benefits, ROI, case studies
```

**B2B:**
```
Primary Strategy: Educational + Personal Outreach
Timing: Slow (24h, 48h, 7d, 14d)
Discount: 10-15% (or no discount)
Channels: Email + Phone
Focus: Value, ROI, relationships
```

### **By Cart Value**

**Low Value ($0-50):**
```
Strategy: Value focus, minimal discount
Timing: Slow track
Discount: 10-12%
Channels: Email only
Priority: Low
```

**Medium Value ($50-200):**
```
Strategy: Balanced approach
Timing: Standard track
Discount: 15-18%
Channels: Email + SMS
Priority: Medium
```

**High Value ($200-500):**
```
Strategy: Premium treatment
Timing: Fast track
Discount: 20-25%
Channels: Email + SMS + Push
Priority: High
```

**Very High Value ($500+):**
```
Strategy: VIP treatment
Timing: Immediate
Discount: 25-30%
Channels: All + Personal
Priority: Highest
```

### **Operational Dashboard**

#### **Email Performance Table**
```
Email | Sent | Opened | Clicked | Converted | Revenue
------|------|--------|---------|-----------|--------
1     | 1000 | 350    | 85      | 45        | $6,750
2     | 955  | 320    | 95      | 60        | $9,000
3     | 895  | 280    | 75      | 50        | $7,500
4     | 845  | 200    | 55      | 40        | $6,000
```

#### **Segment Performance**
```
Segment          | Carts | Recovered | Rate  | Revenue | AOV
-----------------|-------|-----------|-------|---------|-----
High-Value VIP   | 100   | 45        | 45%   | $22,500 | $500
High-Value       | 200   | 60        | 30%   | $18,000 | $300
Standard         | 500   | 100       | 20%   | $15,000 | $150
Low-Value        | 200   | 25        | 12.5% | $2,500  | $100
```

## üé® Complete Visual Design System

### **Color Palette**

#### **Primary Colors**
```
Brand Primary: #007BFF (Blue)
- Use: Primary CTAs, headers, links
- Meaning: Trust, professionalism
- Contrast: 4.5:1 (WCAG AA)

Brand Secondary: #6C757D (Gray)
- Use: Secondary elements, borders
- Meaning: Neutral, professional
- Contrast: 4.5:1 (WCAG AA)
```

#### **Semantic Colors**
```
Success: #28A745 (Green)
- Use: Success messages, savings
- Meaning: Positive, success

Urgency: #DC3545 (Red)
- Use: Urgency, discounts, warnings
- Meaning: Action, urgency

Warning: #FFC107 (Orange)
- Use: Limited offers, special deals
- Meaning: Attention, special

Info: #17A2B8 (Cyan)
- Use: Information, tips
- Meaning: Informational
```

### **Typography Scale**

#### **Font Sizes**
```
H1 (Email Title): 28px, Bold, Line-height: 1.2
H2 (Section): 24px, Bold, Line-height: 1.3
H3 (Subsection): 20px, Semi-bold, Line-height: 1.4
Body: 16px, Regular, Line-height: 1.6
Small: 14px, Regular, Line-height: 1.5
CTA: 18px, Bold, Line-height: 1.2
```

#### **Font Stack**
```
Primary: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif
Fallback: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif
Web Safe: System fonts for email clients
```

### **Spacing System**

#### **Spacing Scale**
```
XS: 4px   - Tight spacing
SM: 8px   - Compact spacing
MD: 16px  - Standard spacing
LG: 24px  - Comfortable spacing
XL: 32px  - Generous spacing
XXL: 48px - Section spacing
```

#### **Component Spacing**
```
Between sections: 32-48px
Between elements: 16-24px
Card padding: 20-24px
CTA padding: 15-20px
Text line height: 1.5-1.6
```

## üí∞ Complete Pricing Strategy Matrix

### **Discount Strategy by Scenario**

#### **Scenario 1: High Competition**
```
Strategy: Aggressive pricing
Email 1: No discount
Email 2: 20% discount
Email 3: 25% discount
Email 4: 30% discount
Focus: Price competitiveness
```

#### **Scenario 2: Premium Brand**
```
Strategy: Value-first, minimal discount
Email 1: No discount
Email 2: 10% discount
Email 3: 15% discount
Email 4: 20% discount
Focus: Brand value, exclusivity
```

#### **Scenario 3: New Product Launch**
```
Strategy: Launch pricing
Email 1: No discount
Email 2: 15% early bird
Email 3: 20% launch offer
Email 4: 25% final launch
Focus: Launch urgency
```

#### **Scenario 4: End of Season**
```
Strategy: Clearance pricing
Email 1: 20% discount
Email 2: 25% discount
Email 3: 30% discount
Email 4: 35% discount
Focus: Clearance urgency
```

### **Dynamic Pricing Rules**

#### **Rule 1: Inventory-Based**
```
IF inventory < 10:
    ‚Üí Add 5% to discount
    ‚Üí Show "Only X left"
    ‚Üí High urgency messaging

IF inventory > 100:
    ‚Üí Standard discount
    ‚Üí Show "In stock"
    ‚Üí Moderate urgency
```

#### **Rule 2: Time-Based**
```
IF time_since_abandon < 24h:
    ‚Üí Lower discount (10-15%)
    ‚Üí Focus on value

IF time_since_abandon > 72h:
    ‚Üí Higher discount (20-25%)
    ‚Üí Focus on urgency
```

#### **Rule 3: Customer-Based**
```
IF customer_segment = "VIP":
    ‚Üí Maximum discount (25-30%)
    ‚Üí Premium treatment

IF customer_segment = "New":
    ‚Üí Welcome discount (15-20%)
    ‚Üí Education focus
```

## üéØ Complete Personalization Matrix

### **Personalization Levels**

#### **Level 1: Basic**
```
Variables:
- First name
- Product name
- Cart total

Example:
"Hi [Name], complete your [Product] purchase for $[Total]"
```

#### **Level 2: Standard**
```
Variables:
- First name
- Product name + category
- Cart total
- Customer segment
- Previous purchases

Example:
"Hi [Name], as a [Segment], complete your [Category] purchase"
```

#### **Level 3: Advanced**
```
Variables:
- First name
- Product details
- Cart total
- Customer segment
- Purchase history
- Engagement level
- Location
- Time of day
- Weather (if relevant)

Example:
"Hi [Name], perfect [Weather] for your [Product]! Complete your $[Total] purchase"
```

#### **Level 4: Hyper-Personalization**
```
Variables:
- All Level 3 variables
- Behavioral data
- Predictive scoring
- Real-time inventory
- Competitor pricing
- Social signals
- Device type
- Previous interactions

Example:
"Hi [Name], based on your [Behavior], we recommend completing your [Product] purchase now. Only [X] left at this price!"
```

## üìà Complete Forecasting Models

### **Revenue Forecast**

#### **Model 1: Simple Linear**
```
Forecast = (Current Recovery Rate √ó Abandoned Carts) √ó AOV

Example:
Recovery Rate: 25%
Abandoned Carts: 1,000/month
AOV: $150

Forecast: (0.25 √ó 1,000) √ó $150 = $37,500/month
```

#### **Model 2: Trend-Based**
```
Forecast = Base Revenue √ó (1 + Growth Rate)^Months

Example:
Base Revenue: $30,000
Growth Rate: 5% per month
Months: 3

Forecast: $30,000 √ó (1.05)^3 = $34,728
```

#### **Model 3: Seasonal Adjustment**
```
Forecast = Base Revenue √ó Seasonal Factor

Example:
Base Revenue: $30,000
Seasonal Factor (Holiday): 1.5

Forecast: $30,000 √ó 1.5 = $45,000
```

### **Recovery Rate Forecast**

#### **Model**
```
Future Rate = Current Rate √ó (1 + Improvement Rate)^Time

Where:
Improvement Rate = Average monthly improvement
Time = Months ahead

Example:
Current Rate: 20%
Improvement Rate: 2% per month
Time: 6 months

Future Rate: 20% √ó (1.02)^6 = 22.5%
```

## üìö Complete Glossary

### **Key Terms**

#### **A/B Testing**
```
Definition: Comparing two versions of an email to determine which performs better
Example: Testing subject line A vs. subject line B
```

#### **Abandonment Rate**
```
Definition: Percentage of carts that are abandoned
Formula: (Abandoned Carts / Total Carts) √ó 100
```

#### **Average Order Value (AOV)**
```
Definition: Average amount spent per order
Formula: Total Revenue / Number of Orders
```

#### **Click-Through Rate (CTR)**
```
Definition: Percentage of recipients who clicked a link
Formula: (Clicks / Emails Sent) √ó 100
```

#### **Conversion Rate**
```
Definition: Percentage of clicks that result in a purchase
Formula: (Purchases / Clicks) √ó 100
```

#### **Customer Lifetime Value (CLV)**
```
Definition: Total value a customer brings over their lifetime
Formula: Average Order Value √ó Purchase Frequency √ó Customer Lifespan
```

#### **Deliverability**
```
Definition: Ability of emails to reach inboxes
Factors: Sender reputation, content, authentication
```

#### **Open Rate**
```
Definition: Percentage of emails opened
Formula: (Opens / Emails Sent) √ó 100
```

#### **Recovery Rate**
```
Definition: Percentage of abandoned carts recovered
Formula: (Recovered Carts / Abandoned Carts) √ó 100
```

#### **Return on Investment (ROI)**
```
Definition: Return on investment in recovery program
Formula: ((Revenue - Costs) / Costs) √ó 100
```

## üìä Complete Metrics Framework

### **Primary Metrics (Track Daily)**

#### **Recovery Metrics**
```
1. Recovery Rate
   Formula: (Recovered / Abandoned) √ó 100
   Target: 20-25%
   Frequency: Daily

2. Revenue Recovered
   Formula: Recovered Carts √ó AOV
   Target: Track vs. goal
   Frequency: Daily

3. Recovery by Email
   Formula: Recovered from Email N / Sent Email N
   Target: Email 2 highest
   Frequency: Daily
```

#### **Engagement Metrics**
```
1. Open Rate
   Formula: (Opens / Sent) √ó 100
   Target: 25-35%
   Frequency: Daily

2. Click Rate
   Formula: (Clicks / Sent) √ó 100
   Target: 5-10%
   Frequency: Daily

3. Click-to-Open Rate
   Formula: (Clicks / Opens) √ó 100
   Target: 15-25%
   Frequency: Daily
```

### **Secondary Metrics (Track Weekly)**

#### **Efficiency Metrics**
```
1. ROI
   Formula: ((Revenue - Costs) / Costs) √ó 100
   Target: 300-500%
   Frequency: Weekly

2. Revenue per Email
   Formula: Revenue / Emails Sent
   Target: $5-15
   Frequency: Weekly

3. Discount Efficiency
   Formula: Revenue / Discount Cost
   Target: 5.0x+
   Frequency: Weekly
```

#### **Quality Metrics**
```
1. Average Order Value
   Formula: Revenue / Orders
   Target: Track vs. baseline
   Frequency: Weekly

2. Customer Lifetime Value
   Formula: AOV √ó Frequency √ó Lifespan
   Target: Track trend
   Frequency: Weekly

3. Unsubscribe Rate
   Formula: (Unsubscribes / Sent) √ó 100
   Target: <0.5%
   Frequency: Weekly
```

### **Advanced Metrics (Track Monthly)**

#### **Predictive Metrics**
```
1. Recovery Probability Score
   Formula: Weighted factors
   Target: Track distribution
   Frequency: Monthly

2. Optimal Discount Prediction
   Formula: ML model
   Target: Maximize ROI
   Frequency: Monthly

3. Churn Risk Score
   Formula: Behavioral analysis
   Target: Identify at-risk
   Frequency: Monthly
```

## üé® Complete Email Component Library

```html
</div>
```

```html
<div class="header" style="text-align: center; padding: 20px;">
    <img src="[LOGO_URL]" alt="[BRAND_NAME]" width="150" style="max-width: 150px;">
    <p style="margin-top: 10px; color: #666; font-size: 14px;">[TAGLINE]</p>
</div>
```

#### **Component 3: Logo + Navigation**
```html
<div class="header" style="text-align: center; padding: 20px; border-bottom: 1px solid #e0e0e0;">

    <div style="margin-top: 15px;">
        <a href="[SHOP_URL]" style="margin: 0 10px; color: #007bff; text-decoration: none;">Shop</a>
        <a href="[ABOUT_URL]" style="margin: 0 10px; color: #007bff; text-decoration: none;">About</a>
        <a href="[CONTACT_URL]" style="margin: 0 10px; color: #007bff; text-decoration: none;">Contact</a>
    </div>
</div>
```

```html
</div>
```

```html
<div class="product-card" style="border: 1px solid #e0e0e0; border-radius: 8px; padding: 20px; margin: 20px 0;">

    <p style="margin: 0 0 10px 0; color: #666;">[PRODUCT_DESCRIPTION]</p>
    <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold;">$[PRICE] √ó [QUANTITY]</p>
</div>
```

#### **Component 3: Product Grid**
```html
<table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
    <tr>
        <td width="50%" style="padding: 10px;">
            <img src="[PRODUCT_1_IMAGE]" alt="[PRODUCT_1_NAME]" width="100%" style="max-width: 100%;">
            <h4>[PRODUCT_1_NAME]</h4>
            <p>$[PRODUCT_1_PRICE]</p>

            <h4>[PRODUCT_2_NAME]</h4>
            <p>$[PRODUCT_2_PRICE]</p>
        </td>
    </tr>
</table>
```

### **CTA Components**

#### **Component 1: Primary Button**
```html
<div style="text-align: center; margin: 30px 0;">
    <a href="[CTA_URL]" style="display: inline-block; padding: 15px 30px; background-color: #007bff; color: #ffffff; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 18px;">[CTA_TEXT]</a>
</div>
```

#### **Component 2: Secondary Button**
```html
<div style="text-align: center; margin: 30px 0;">
    <a href="[CTA_URL]" style="display: inline-block; padding: 15px 30px; border: 2px solid #007bff; color: #007bff; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 18px;">[CTA_TEXT]</a>
</div>
```

#### **Component 3: Text Link**
```html
<div style="text-align: center; margin: 30px 0;">
    <a href="[CTA_URL]" style="color: #007bff; text-decoration: underline; font-size: 16px;">[CTA_TEXT]</a>
</div>
```

## üöÄ Complete Automation Scripts

### **JavaScript: Cart Tracking**

#### **Complete Tracking Script**
```javascript
// Complete cart abandonment tracking
(function() {
    'use strict';
    
    const CartTracker = {
        config: {
            trackingInterval: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutes
            apiEndpoint: '/api/cart/track',
            storageKey: 'cart_data'
        },
        
        cartData: null,
        inactivityTimer: null,
        
        init: function() {
            this.loadCartData();
            this.setupEventListeners();
            this.startTracking();
        },
        
        loadCartData: function() {
            const saved = localStorage.getItem(this.config.storageKey);
            if (saved) {
                this.cartData = JSON.parse(saved);
            }
        },
        
        setupEventListeners: function() {
            // Track cart updates
            document.addEventListener('cart:updated', (e) => {
                this.updateCart(e.detail);
            });
            
            // Track user activity
            ['mousemove', 'keypress', 'scroll', 'touchstart', 'click'].forEach(event => {
                document.addEventListener(event, () => this.resetTimer(), { passive: true });
            });
            
            // Track page visibility
            document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', () => {
                if (document.hidden) {
                    this.checkAbandonment();
                }
            });
            
            // Track exit intent
            document.addEventListener('mouseleave', (e) => {
                if (e.clientY <= 0) {
                    this.trackExitIntent();
                }
            });
        },
        
        updateCart: function(cart) {
            if (cart.items && cart.items.length > 0) {
                this.cartData = {
                    cartId: this.generateCartId(),
                    email: this.getEmail(),
                    firstName: this.getFirstName(),
                    items: cart.items,
                    total: cart.total,
                    timestamp: Date.now(),
                    sessionId: this.getSessionId()
                };
                this.saveCart();
                this.resetTimer();
            }
        },
        
        checkAbandonment: function() {
            if (this.cartData && !this.isCheckoutPage()) {
                const timeSinceUpdate = Date.now() - this.cartData.timestamp;
                if (timeSinceUpdate >= this.config.trackingInterval) {
                    this.trackAbandonment();
                }
            }
        },
        
        trackAbandonment: function() {
            if (!this.cartData || this.cartData.abandoned) return;
            
            fetch(this.config.apiEndpoint, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    event: 'cart_abandoned',
                    data: this.cartData
                })
            }).then(response => {
                if (response.ok) {
                    this.cartData.abandoned = true;
                    this.saveCart();
                }
            }).catch(error => {
                console.error('Tracking error:', error);
            });
        },
        
        trackExitIntent: function() {
            if (this.cartData && !this.isCheckoutPage()) {
                fetch(this.config.apiEndpoint, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        event: 'exit_intent',
                        data: {
                            cartId: this.cartData.cartId,
                            cartValue: this.cartData.total,
                            timestamp: Date.now()
                        }
                    })
                });
            }
        },
        
        getEmail: function() {
            return document.querySelector('[data-email]')?.value ||
                   localStorage.getItem('user_email') ||
                   this.getEmailFromForm();
        },
        
        getEmailFromForm: function() {
            const emailInput = document.querySelector('input[type="email"]');
            return emailInput?.value || null;
        },
        
        getFirstName: function() {
            return document.querySelector('[data-first-name]')?.value ||
                   localStorage.getItem('user_first_name') ||
                   null;
        },
        
        getSessionId: function() {
            let sessionId = sessionStorage.getItem('session_id');
            if (!sessionId) {
                sessionId = this.generateSessionId();
                sessionStorage.setItem('session_id', sessionId);
            }
            return sessionId;
        },
        
        generateCartId: function() {
            return 'cart_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);
        },
        
        generateSessionId: function() {
            return 'session_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);
        },
        
        isCheckoutPage: function() {
            return window.location.pathname.includes('checkout') ||
                   window.location.pathname.includes('payment');
        },
        
        saveCart: function() {
            if (this.cartData) {
                localStorage.setItem(this.config.storageKey, JSON.stringify(this.cartData));
            }
        },
        
        resetTimer: function() {
            clearTimeout(this.inactivityTimer);
            this.inactivityTimer = setTimeout(() => {
                this.checkAbandonment();
            }, this.config.trackingInterval);
        },
        
        startTracking: function() {
            this.resetTimer();
        }
    };
    
    // Initialize when DOM is ready
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => CartTracker.init());
    } else {
        CartTracker.init();
    }
})();
```

## üéØ Complete Testing Playbook

### **A/B Testing Calendar**

#### **Month 1: Foundation Tests**
```
Week 1: Subject Lines
  Test: With vs. Without Personalization
  Variants: 2
  Sample: 2,000 per variant
  Duration: 7 days

Week 2: CTA Text
  Test: Action-focused vs. Benefit-focused
  Variants: 2
  Sample: 1,500 per variant
  Duration: 7 days

Week 3: Discount Levels
  Test: 15% vs. 20% vs. 25%
  Variants: 3
  Sample: 1,000 per variant
  Duration: 14 days

Week 4: Send Times
  Test: Morning vs. Afternoon vs. Evening
  Variants: 3
  Sample: 1,000 per variant
  Duration: 14 days
```

#### **Month 2: Content Tests**
```
Week 1: Email Length
  Test: Short vs. Medium vs. Long
  Variants: 3
  Sample: 1,000 per variant
  Duration: 14 days

Week 2: Image vs. Text
  Test: Image-heavy vs. Text-heavy
  Variants: 2
  Sample: 1,500 per variant
  Duration: 14 days

Week 3: Personalization Level
  Test: Basic vs. Advanced
  Variants: 2
  Sample: 2,000 per variant
  Duration: 14 days

Week 4: Urgency Messaging
  Test: High vs. Moderate vs. Low
  Variants: 3
  Sample: 1,000 per variant
  Duration: 14 days
```

#### **Month 3: Advanced Tests**
```
Week 1: Multi-variate (Subject + CTA)
  Test: 4 combinations
  Variants: 4
  Sample: 1,000 per variant
  Duration: 14 days

Week 2: Discount Presentation
  Test: Percentage vs. Dollar amount vs. Both
  Variants: 3
  Sample: 1,000 per variant
  Duration: 14 days

Week 3: Social Proof Placement
  Test: Top vs. Middle vs. Bottom
  Variants: 3
  Sample: 1,000 per variant
  Duration: 14 days

Week 4: Trust Elements
  Test: With vs. Without trust badges
  Variants: 2
  Sample: 2,000 per variant
  Duration: 14 days
```

## üéÅ Complete Incentive Library

### **Discount Codes**

#### **Format 1: Simple**
```
CART[PERCENTAGE]
Example: CART20 (20% off)
```

#### **Format 2: Time-Based**
```
CART[PERCENTAGE][DATE]
Example: CART20JAN (20% off, expires Jan 31)
```

#### **Format 3: Customer-Specific**
```
[CUSTOMER_ID][PERCENTAGE]
Example: CUST12320 (Customer 123, 20% off)
```

### **Non-Discount Incentives**

#### **Free Shipping**
```
Message: "Free shipping on orders over $[AMOUNT]"
Value: $[SHIPPING_COST]
Best For: Low to medium value carts
```

#### **Free Gift**
```
Message: "Free [GIFT_NAME] with your order (Value: $[VALUE])"
Value: $[GIFT_VALUE]
Best For: Medium to high value carts
```

#### **Extended Warranty**
```
Message: "Free extended warranty (Value: $[VALUE])"
Value: $[WARRANTY_VALUE]
Best For: Electronics, high-value items
```

#### **Early Access**
```
Message: "Early access to [NEW_COLLECTION/PRODUCT]"
Value: Exclusivity
Best For: Fashion, limited editions
```

#### **Personal Service**
```
Message: "Free personal shopping assistance"
Value: Premium experience
Best For: High-value, VIP customers
```

## üéØ Complete Success Framework

### **Success Metrics by Goal**

#### **Goal 1: Maximize Recovery Rate**
```
Primary Metric: Recovery Rate
Target: 25-30%
Secondary Metrics:
- Email open rate: 30%+
- Email click rate: 8%+
- Conversion rate: 15%+

Key Strategies:
- Optimize subject lines
- Improve email content
- Test discount levels
- Refine timing
- Enhance personalization

Success Indicators:
- Recovery rate increasing monthly
- All emails performing well
- High engagement rates
```

#### **Goal 2: Maximize Revenue**
```
Primary Metric: Revenue Recovered
Target: Track vs. goal
Secondary Metrics:
- Average order value: Track vs. baseline
- Revenue per email: $10+
- Total revenue: Track monthly

Key Strategies:
- Focus on high-value carts
- Increase AOV with upsells
- Optimize discount strategy
- Target high-value segments

Success Indicators:
- Revenue increasing monthly
- AOV maintained or increased
- High-value segment performing
```

#### **Goal 3: Maximize ROI**
```
Primary Metric: ROI
Target: 400-500%+
Secondary Metrics:
- Discount efficiency: 5.0x+
- Cost per recovery: Minimize
- Net revenue: Maximize

Key Strategies:
- Reduce discount dependency
- Optimize discount levels
- Improve recovery rate
- Reduce costs

Success Indicators:
- ROI increasing monthly
- Discount efficiency improving
- Costs controlled
```

#### **Goal 4: Build Customer Relationships**
```
Primary Metric: Customer Satisfaction
Target: High satisfaction
Secondary Metrics:
- Repeat purchase rate: Track
- Customer lifetime value: Track
- Referral rate: Track
- Unsubscribe rate: <0.5%

Key Strategies:
- Value-first approach
- Educational content
- Trust building
- Personalization

Success Indicators:
- Low unsubscribe rate
- High repeat purchases
- Positive feedback
- Growing CLV
```

## üìä Complete Analytics Implementation

### **Google Analytics 4 Setup**

#### **Event Configuration**
```javascript
// Track cart abandonment
gtag('event', 'cart_abandoned', {
    'event_category': 'Ecommerce',
    'event_label': 'Cart Abandonment',
    'value': cartTotal,
    'currency': 'USD',
    'items': cartItems.map(item => ({
        'item_id': item.id,
        'item_name': item.name,
        'price': item.price,
        'quantity': item.quantity,
        'item_category': item.category
    }))
});

// Track email sent
gtag('event', 'email_sent', {
    'event_category': 'Email',
    'event_label': 'Abandoned Cart Email',
    'email_number': emailNumber,
    'email_type': emailType,
    'cart_value': cartValue
});

// Track email opened
gtag('event', 'email_opened', {
    'event_category': 'Email',
    'event_label': 'Abandoned Cart Email Opened',
    'email_number': emailNumber,
    'email_type': emailType
});

// Track email clicked
gtag('event', 'email_clicked', {
    'event_category': 'Email',
    'event_label': 'Abandoned Cart Email Clicked',
    'email_number': emailNumber,
    'email_type': emailType,
    'link_url': linkUrl
});

// Track recovery
gtag('event', 'cart_recovered', {
    'event_category': 'Ecommerce',
    'event_label': 'Cart Recovered',
    'value': orderTotal,
    'currency': 'USD',
    'email_number': emailNumber,
    'transaction_id': orderId
});
```

### **Custom Dimensions**

#### **Recommended Dimensions**
```
1. Customer Segment
   - Values: New, Returning, VIP
   - Use: Segmentation analysis

2. Cart Value Tier
   - Values: Low, Medium, High, Very High
   - Use: Value-based analysis

3. Product Category
   - Values: Category names
   - Use: Category performance

4. Email Number
   - Values: 1, 2, 3, 4
   - Use: Email performance

5. Discount Level
   - Values: None, 10%, 15%, 20%, 25%+
   - Use: Discount analysis
```

### **Color Schemes**

#### **Scheme 1: Professional Blue**
```
Primary: #007BFF (Blue)
Secondary: #6C757D (Gray)
Accent: #28A745 (Green)
Background: #FFFFFF
Text: #212529
```

#### **Scheme 2: Energetic Orange**
```
Primary: #FF6B35 (Orange)
Secondary: #004E89 (Navy)
Accent: #FFC107 (Yellow)
Background: #FFFFFF
Text: #212529
```

#### **Scheme 3: Elegant Purple**
```

Accent: #00B894 (Teal)
```

## üöÄ Complete Integration Guide

### **Shopify Integration**

#### **Liquid Template**
```liquid
<!-- Cart abandonment tracking -->
<script>
  window.abandonedCart = {
    email: '{{ customer.email }}',
    firstName: '{{ customer.first_name }}',
    cartItems: [
      {% for item in cart.items %}
      {
        id: {{ item.product_id }},
        variantId: {{ item.variant_id }},
        name: '{{ item.product.title | escape }}',
        price: {{ item.price }},
        quantity: {{ item.quantity }},
        image: '{{ item.image | img_url: 'medium' }}',
        url: '{{ item.product.url }}'
      }{% unless forloop.last %},{% endunless %}
      {% endfor %}
    ],
    cartTotal: {{ cart.total_price }},
    itemCount: {{ cart.item_count }}
  };
  
  // Track cart abandonment
  if (window.abandonedCart.cartItems.length > 0) {
    // Send to your tracking endpoint
    fetch('/api/cart/track', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
      body: JSON.stringify(window.abandonedCart)
    });
  }
</script>
```

### **WooCommerce Integration**

#### **PHP Hook**
```php
// Track cart abandonment
add_action('woocommerce_add_to_cart', 'track_cart_update', 10, 6);
add_action('woocommerce_cart_item_removed', 'track_cart_update', 10, 2);

function track_cart_update() {
    $cart = WC()->cart;
    $cart_items = array();
    
    foreach ($cart->get_cart() as $cart_item_key => $cart_item) {
        $product = $cart_item['data'];
        $cart_items[] = array(
            'id' => $product->get_id(),
            'name' => $product->get_name(),
            'price' => $product->get_price(),
            'quantity' => $cart_item['quantity'],
            'image' => wp_get_attachment_image_url($product->get_image_id(), 'medium'),
            'url' => $product->get_permalink()
        );
    }
    
    $cart_data = array(
        'email' => is_user_logged_in() ? wp_get_current_user()->user_email : null,
        'firstName' => is_user_logged_in() ? wp_get_current_user()->first_name : null,
        'cartItems' => $cart_items,
        'cartTotal' => $cart->get_total(''),
        'itemCount' => $cart->get_cart_contents_count(),
        'timestamp' => time()
    );
    
    // Store in transient for tracking
    set_transient('abandoned_cart_' . session_id(), $cart_data, 7 * DAY_IN_SECONDS);
}
```

### **Klaviyo Integration**

#### **JavaScript Tracking**
```javascript
// Track abandoned cart
_learnq.push(['track', 'Abandoned Cart', {
    '$value': cartTotal,
    'Items': cartItems.map(item => ({
        'ProductID': item.id,
        'SKU': item.sku,
        'ProductName': item.name,
        'Price': item.price,
        'Quantity': item.quantity,
        'ImageURL': item.image,
        'ProductURL': item.url
    }))
}]);

// Track email engagement
_learnq.push(['track', 'Email Opened', {
    'Email Type': 'Abandoned Cart',
    'Email Number': emailNumber,
    'Cart Value': cartValue
}]);

// Track recovery
_learnq.push(['track', 'Placed Order', {
    '$value': orderTotal,
    '$event_id': orderId,
    'Items': orderItems,
    'Abandoned Cart Recovered': true,
    'Recovery Email Number': emailNumber
}]);
```

```

- Audit logging
```

```
- Collect only necessary data
- Delete unused data
- Anonymize when possible
- Regular cleanup

- Clear consent requests
- Easy opt-out
- Consent tracking
- Regular reviews
```

## üìä Complete Advanced Analytics

### **Attribution Modeling**

#### **Model 1: First-Touch Attribution**
```
Credit: First email that customer engaged with
Use: Understanding initial interest
Example: Email 1 opened ‚Üí Credit to Email 1
```

#### **Model 2: Last-Touch Attribution**
```
Credit: Last email before purchase
Use: Understanding final conversion
Example: Email 3 clicked ‚Üí Credit to Email 3
```

#### **Model 3: Linear Attribution**
```
Credit: Equal credit to all emails
Use: Understanding full journey
Example: 4 emails sent ‚Üí 25% credit each
```

#### **Model 4: Time-Decay Attribution**
```
Credit: More credit to recent emails
Use: Understanding recency impact
Example: Email 4: 40%, Email 3: 30%, Email 2: 20%, Email 1: 10%
```

#### **Model 5: Position-Based Attribution**
```
Credit: 40% first, 40% last, 20% middle
Use: Understanding key touchpoints
Example: Email 1: 40%, Email 2-3: 10% each, Email 4: 40%
```

### **Cohort Analysis**

#### **Cohort Definition**
```
Cohort 1: Customers who abandoned in Week 1
Cohort 2: Customers who abandoned in Week 2
Cohort 3: Customers who abandoned in Week 3
...and so on
```

#### **Analysis Metrics**
```
Recovery Rate by Cohort:
- Week 1 Cohort: [X]%
- Week 2 Cohort: [X]%
- Week 3 Cohort: [X]%

Revenue by Cohort:
- Week 1 Cohort: $[X]
- Week 2 Cohort: $[X]
- Week 3 Cohort: $[X]

Trend Analysis:
- Improving over time?
- Declining over time?
- Stable performance?
```

## üöÄ Complete Advanced Automation

### **AI-Powered Personalization**

#### **Machine Learning Models**

#### **Model 1: Send Time Optimization**
```python
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
import pandas as pd

def train_send_time_model(historical_data):
    """
    Train model to predict optimal send time
    """
    # Features
    X = historical_data[['hour', 'day_of_week', 'customer_segment', 
                         'product_category', 'cart_value']]
    
    # Target: Best send time (hour with highest open rate)
    y = historical_data['optimal_send_hour']
    
    # Train model
    model = RandomForestClassifier()
    model.fit(X, y)
    
    return model

def predict_optimal_send_time(customer_data, model):
    """
    Predict optimal send time for customer
    """
    prediction = model.predict([customer_data])
    return prediction[0]
```

#### **Model 2: Discount Optimization**
```python
from sklearn.ensemble import GradientBoostingRegressor

def train_discount_model(historical_data):
    """
    Train model to predict optimal discount
    """
    # Features
    X = historical_data[['cart_value', 'customer_segment', 
                         'time_since_abandon', 'product_category',
                         'previous_discounts', 'engagement_level']]
    
    # Target: Discount that maximizes ROI
    y = historical_data['optimal_discount']
    
    # Train model
    model = GradientBoostingRegressor()
    model.fit(X, y)
    
    return model

def predict_optimal_discount(cart_data, model):
    """
    Predict optimal discount for cart
    """
    prediction = model.predict([cart_data])
    return min(max(prediction[0], 10), 30)  # Cap between 10-30%
```

#### **Model 3: Recovery Probability Score**
```python
from sklearn.ensemble import GradientBoostingClassifier

def train_recovery_model(historical_data):
    """
    Train model to predict recovery probability
    """
    # Features
    X = historical_data[['cart_value', 'customer_segment',
                         'time_since_abandon', 'engagement_level',
                         'product_category', 'previous_purchases',
                         'email_open_rate', 'email_click_rate']]
    
    # Target: Will recover (1) or not (0)
    y = historical_data['recovered']
    
    # Train model
    model = GradientBoostingClassifier()
    model.fit(X, y)
    
    return model

def predict_recovery_probability(cart_data, model):
    """
    Predict recovery probability (0-100)
    """
    probability = model.predict_proba([cart_data])[0][1]
    return probability * 100
```

## üõ†Ô∏è Complete Technical Optimization

### **Email Performance Optimization**

#### **Image Optimization**
```
Best Practices:
- Format: JPEG for photos, PNG for graphics
- Size: Max 200KB per image
- Dimensions: 600px width max
- Compression: 80-85% quality
- Alt text: Descriptive and helpful
- Lazy loading: For multiple images

Tools:
- TinyPNG: Compression
- Squoosh: Advanced compression
- ImageOptim: Batch optimization
```

#### **Code Optimization**
```
HTML:
- Minimize code
- Remove comments
- Inline CSS
- Table-based layout
- Avoid external stylesheets

CSS:
- Inline styles
- Media queries (limited)
- Avoid advanced selectors
- Test across clients

JavaScript:
- Minimal use
- Progressive enhancement
- Fallbacks
- Test thoroughly
```

### **Deliverability Optimization**

#### **Authentication**
```
SPF Record:
v=spf1 include:_spf.example.com ~all

DKIM Record:
v=DKIM1; k=rsa; p=[public key]

DMARC Policy:
v=DMARC1; p=quarantine; rua=mailto:dmarc@example.com
```

#### **Reputation Management**
```
Monitor:
- Sender score
- Blacklist status
- Complaint rates
- Bounce rates

Maintain:
- Clean list
- Regular sending
- Good engagement
- Proper authentication
```

## üéÅ Complete Advanced Incentive Strategies

### **Dynamic Incentive System**

#### **System Architecture**
```
Cart Abandoned
    ‚Üì
Analyze Cart
    ‚Üì
Calculate Incentive Score
    ‚Üì
Select Optimal Incentive
    ‚Üì
Factors Considered:
- Cart value
- Customer segment
- Time since abandon
- Inventory level
- Customer history
- Engagement level
- Product category
    ‚Üì
Apply Incentive
```

#### **Incentive Types**

#### **Type 1: Percentage Discount**
```
Calculation:
Base: 10%
+ Cart value factor: 0-5%
+ Customer segment: 0-3%
+ Time factor: 0-2%
+ Inventory factor: 0-2%
= Total discount (capped at 30%)

Example:
Cart: $200, Returning customer, 48h, Low stock
Discount: 10% + 3% + 2% + 2% = 17%
```

#### **Type 2: Dollar Amount Discount**
```
Calculation:
Base: $10
+ Cart value factor: 0-5% of value
+ Customer segment: 0-3% of value
= Total discount

Example:
Cart: $200, VIP customer
Discount: $10 + $10 + $6 = $26
```

#### **Type 3: Free Shipping**
```
Threshold: Dynamic based on cart value
Calculation:
IF cart_value < $50:
    ‚Üí Offer free shipping if reach $50
ELIF cart_value < $100:
    ‚Üí Offer free shipping if reach $100
ELSE:
    ‚Üí Free shipping included
```

#### **Type 4: Free Gift**
```
Selection:
- Based on cart value
- Based on product category
- Based on customer segment

Examples:
- Low value: Small gift ($5-10)
- Medium value: Standard gift ($10-25)
- High value: Premium gift ($25-50)
```

## üéØ Complete Customer Psychology 2.0

### **Advanced Psychological Triggers**

#### **1. The Decoy Effect**
```
Principle: Adding a third option makes one option more attractive
Application:
- Show 3 options: Basic, Standard, Premium
- Make Standard the "sweet spot"
- Most customers choose Standard

Example:
Option A: $50 (Basic)
Option B: $75 (Standard) ‚Üê Recommended
Option C: $100 (Premium)
```

#### **2. The Endowment Effect**
```
Principle: People value things more when they own them
Application:
- "Your cart" language
- "Your items" messaging
- "Reserved for you"
- Personal ownership

Example:
"Your cart is waiting"
"Your items are reserved"
"Your perfect [Product]"
```

#### **3. The Framing Effect**
```
Principle: How information is presented affects decisions
Application:
- Frame discounts as savings
- Frame urgency as opportunity
- Frame value as investment
- Positive framing

Example:
"Save $50" vs "Pay $150"
"Limited time" vs "Available now"
"Investment" vs "Cost"
```

#### **4. The Anchoring Effect**
```
Principle: First number seen influences perception
Application:
- Show original price first
- Then show discount
- Emphasize savings
- Create value perception

Example:
Original: $200
Your Price: $150
You Save: $50
```

#### **5. The Reciprocity Principle**
```
Principle: People feel obligated to return favors
Application:
- Give value first
- Offer help
- Provide information
- Then ask for purchase

Example:
"Here's a free guide"
"Free consultation"
"Expert advice"
"Then: Complete your purchase"
```

---

## üõ†Ô∏è Complete Technical Implementation 2.0

### **Advanced Tracking Implementation**

#### **Complete Event Tracking**
```javascript
// Complete event tracking system
class AdvancedEventTracker {
    constructor() {
        this.events = [];
        this.config = {
            apiEndpoint: '/api/events',
            batchSize: 10,
            flushInterval: 5000
        };
        this.init();
    }
    
    init() {
        this.setupEventListeners();
        this.startFlushTimer();
    }
    
    setupEventListeners() {
        // Track cart events
        document.addEventListener('cart:updated', (e) => {
            this.track('cart_updated', e.detail);
        });
        
        document.addEventListener('cart:abandoned', (e) => {
            this.track('cart_abandoned', e.detail);
        });
        
        // Track email events
        document.addEventListener('email:opened', (e) => {
            this.track('email_opened', e.detail);
        });
        
        document.addEventListener('email:clicked', (e) => {
            this.track('email_clicked', e.detail);
        });
        
        // Track recovery events
        document.addEventListener('cart:recovered', (e) => {
            this.track('cart_recovered', e.detail);
        });
    }
    
    track(eventName, data) {
        const event = {
            name: eventName,
            data: data,
            timestamp: Date.now(),
            sessionId: this.getSessionId(),
            userId: this.getUserId()
        };
        
        this.events.push(event);
        
        // Flush if batch size reached
        if (this.events.length >= this.config.batchSize) {
            this.flush();
        }
    }
    
    flush() {
        if (this.events.length === 0) return;
        
        const eventsToSend = [...this.events];
        this.events = [];
        
        fetch(this.config.apiEndpoint, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json'
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                events: eventsToSend
            })
        }).catch(error => {
            console.error('Event tracking error:', error);
            // Re-add events to queue on error
            this.events.unshift(...eventsToSend);
        });
    }
    
    startFlushTimer() {
        setInterval(() => {
            this.flush();
        }, this.config.flushInterval);
    }
    
    getSessionId() {
        let sessionId = sessionStorage.getItem('session_id');
        if (!sessionId) {
            sessionId = 'session_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);
            sessionStorage.setItem('session_id', sessionId);
        }
        return sessionId;
    }
    
    getUserId() {
        return localStorage.getItem('user_id') || null;
    }
}

// Initialize
const eventTracker = new AdvancedEventTracker();
```

## üìä Complete Data Analysis Framework

### **Statistical Analysis**

#### **Correlation Analysis**
```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from scipy import stats

def analyze_correlations(data):
    """
    Analyze correlations between variables and recovery
    """
    # Variables to analyze
    variables = ['cart_value', 'customer_segment', 'time_since_abandon',
                 'email_open_rate', 'email_click_rate', 'discount_level']
    
    correlations = {}
    for var in variables:
        corr, p_value = stats.pearsonr(data[var], data['recovered'])
        correlations[var] = {
            'correlation': corr,
            'p_value': p_value,
            'significant': p_value < 0.05
        }
    
    return correlations
```

#### **Regression Analysis**
```python
from sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression
from sklearn.metrics import r2_score

def predict_recovery(data):
    """
    Predict recovery using regression
    """
    # Features
    X = data[['cart_value', 'customer_segment', 'time_since_abandon',
              'email_open_rate', 'email_click_rate', 'discount_level']]
    
    # Target
    y = data['recovered']
    
    # Train model
    model = LinearRegression()
    model.fit(X, y)
    
    # Predictions
    predictions = model.predict(X)
    r2 = r2_score(y, predictions)
    
    return {
        'model': model,
        'r2_score': r2,
        'coefficients': model.coef_,
        'predictions': predictions
    }
```

## üéØ Complete Advanced Copywriting Mastery

### **Power Words Library**

#### **Urgency Words**
```
- Now
- Today
- Limited
- Expires
- Final
- Last chance
- Don't miss
- Hurry
- Soon
- Urgent
```

#### **Value Words**
```
- Save
- Free
- Bonus
- Exclusive
- Special
- Premium
- Value
- Deal
- Offer
- Discount
```

#### **Trust Words**
```
- Guaranteed
- Secure
- Trusted
- Verified
- Certified
- Safe
- Reliable
- Proven
- Established
- Credible
```

#### **Emotional Words**
```
- Love
- Perfect
- Amazing
- Incredible
- Transform
- Discover
- Experience
- Enjoy
- Delight
- Thrilled
```

### **Copywriting Formulas Expanded**

#### **Formula 4: STAR (Situation, Task, Action, Result)**
```
SITUATION: You left [Product] in your cart
TASK: Complete your purchase
ACTION: Use your [X]% discount code
RESULT: Get [Product] + save $[Amount]

Example:
"You left [Product] in your cart. Complete your purchase now using 
your 20% discount code and get [Product] + save $50."
```

#### **Formula 5: 4U's (Useful, Urgent, Unique, Ultra-specific)**
```
USEFUL: Information that helps the customer
URGENT: Time-sensitive element
UNIQUE: What makes this special
ULTRA-SPECIFIC: Specific details

Example:
"Complete your $250 cart and save $50 (20% off) - Offer expires in 24 hours. 
This discount is exclusive to you and won't be available again."
```

#### **Formula 6: Problem-Agitate-Solve-Benefit (PASB)**
```
PROBLEM: [Identify the problem]
AGITATE: [Make it worse]
SOLVE: [Offer solution]
BENEFIT: [Show the benefit]

Example:
"You need [Product] but haven't completed your purchase. Every day without 
[Product] means missing out on [Benefit]. Complete your purchase now and 
get [Product] + 20% off. You'll enjoy [Benefit] immediately."
```

## üé® Complete Advanced Design System 3.0

### **Accessibility Guidelines**

#### **WCAG Compliance**
```
Level AA Requirements:
‚úÖ Color contrast: 4.5:1 minimum
‚úÖ Text size: 16px minimum
‚úÖ Alt text: All images
‚úÖ Keyboard navigation: Supported
‚úÖ Screen reader: Compatible
‚úÖ Focus indicators: Visible
```

#### **Color Contrast Calculator**
```javascript
function calculateContrast(color1, color2) {
    // Convert to RGB
    const rgb1 = hexToRgb(color1);
    const rgb2 = hexToRgb(color2);
    
    // Calculate relative luminance
    const l1 = getLuminance(rgb1);
    const l2 = getLuminance(rgb2);
    
    // Calculate contrast ratio
    const ratio = (Math.max(l1, l2) + 0.05) / (Math.min(l1, l2) + 0.05);
    
    return {
        ratio: ratio,
        aa: ratio >= 4.5,
        aaa: ratio >= 7
    };
}
```

### **Dark Mode Implementation**

#### **Complete Dark Mode CSS**
```css
@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark) {
    body {
        background-color: #1a1a1a !important;
        color: #ffffff !important;
    }
    
    .container {
        background-color: #2d2d2d !important;
    }
    
    .header {
        background-color: #2d2d2d !important;
        border-bottom: 1px solid #404040 !important;
    }
    
    .content {
        color: #e0e0e0 !important;
    }
    
    .product-card {
        background-color: #2d2d2d !important;
        border: 1px solid #404040 !important;
    }
    
    .cta-button {
        background-color: #007bff !important;
        color: #ffffff !important;
    }
    
    a {
        color: #4da6ff !important;
    }
    
    .footer {
        background-color: #1a1a1a !important;
        color: #999999 !important;
    }
}
```

## üöÄ Complete Advanced Automation 2.0

### **AI-Powered Content Generation**

#### **Subject Line Generator**
```python
import openai

def generate_subject_lines(cart_data, num_variants=5):
    """
    Generate personalized subject lines using AI
    """
    prompt = f"""
    Generate {num_variants} email subject lines for abandoned cart recovery.
    
    Context:
    - Customer name: {cart_data['firstName']}
    - Product: {cart_data['productName']}
    - Cart value: ${cart_data['total']}
    - Discount: {cart_data['discount']}%
    - Time since abandon: {cart_data['hours']} hours
    
    Requirements:
    - Personal and engaging
    - Create urgency
    - Include value proposition
    - Under 50 characters
    - Mobile-friendly
    """
    
    response = openai.Completion.create(
        engine="text-davinci-003",
        prompt=prompt,
        max_tokens=200,
        temperature=0.7
    )
    
    return response.choices[0].text.strip().split('\n')
```

#### **Email Copy Generator**
```python
def generate_email_copy(cart_data, email_number):
    """
    Generate personalized email copy using AI
    """
    templates = {
        1: "reminder",
        2: "value",
        3: "discount",
        4: "final"
    }
    
    prompt = f"""
    Write an abandoned cart recovery email.
    
    Type: {templates[email_number]}
    Customer: {cart_data['firstName']}
    Product: {cart_data['productName']}
    Cart value: ${cart_data['total']}
    Discount: {cart_data['discount']}%
    
    Tone: Friendly, helpful, urgent
    Length: 150-200 words
    Include: Personalization, value, CTA
    """
    
    response = openai.Completion.create(
        engine="text-davinci-003",
        prompt=prompt,
        max_tokens=300,
        temperature=0.7
    )
    
    return response.choices[0].text.strip()
```

## üìà Complete Revenue Forecasting 2.0

### **Advanced Forecasting Models**

#### **Model 4: Machine Learning Forecast**
```python
from sklearn.ensemble import GradientBoostingRegressor
import pandas as pd

def ml_revenue_forecast(historical_data, future_periods=30):
    """
    Forecast revenue using machine learning
    """
    # Prepare features
    features = ['day_of_week', 'month', 'season', 'promotion_active',
                'historical_recovery_rate', 'historical_abandoned_carts']
    
    X = historical_data[features]
    y = historical_data['revenue_recovered']
    
    # Train model
    model = GradientBoostingRegressor(n_estimators=100, learning_rate=0.1)
    model.fit(X, y)
    
    # Generate future features
    future_data = generate_future_features(future_periods)
    
    # Predict
    predictions = model.predict(future_data)
    
    return {
        'predictions': predictions,
        'total_forecast': sum(predictions),
        'confidence_intervals': calculate_confidence_intervals(predictions)
    }
```

#### **Model 5: Ensemble Forecast**
```python
def ensemble_forecast(historical_data):
    """
    Combine multiple forecasting models
    """
    # Model 1: Linear trend
    linear_forecast = linear_trend_forecast(historical_data)
    
    # Model 2: Seasonal adjustment
    seasonal_forecast = seasonal_forecast(historical_data)
    
    # Model 3: ML model
    ml_forecast = ml_revenue_forecast(historical_data)
    
    # Weighted average
    weights = [0.3, 0.3, 0.4]  # ML gets more weight
    ensemble = (linear_forecast * weights[0] + 
                seasonal_forecast * weights[1] + 
                ml_forecast * weights[2])
    
    return ensemble
```

## üéØ Complete Advanced Personalization 3.0

### **Real-Time Personalization**

#### **Dynamic Content Engine**
```python
def generate_personalized_content(customer_data, cart_data):
    """
    Generate fully personalized email content
    """
    personalization = {
        'greeting': personalize_greeting(customer_data),
        'product_recommendations': get_recommendations(cart_data),
        'discount': calculate_optimal_discount(cart_data),
        'urgency_level': calculate_urgency(cart_data),
        'social_proof': get_relevant_social_proof(cart_data),
        'trust_elements': get_trust_elements(customer_data),
        'cta_text': personalize_cta(customer_data, cart_data)
    }
    
    return personalization

def personalize_greeting(customer_data):
    """
    Personalize greeting based on time, location, history
    """
    hour = datetime.now().hour
    location = customer_data.get('location', 'unknown')
    
    if 6 <= hour < 12:
        return f"Good morning, {customer_data['firstName']}!"
    elif 12 <= hour < 18:
        return f"Good afternoon, {customer_data['firstName']}!"
    else:
        return f"Good evening, {customer_data['firstName']}!"
```

### **Behavioral Personalization**

#### **Content Based on Behavior**
```python
def personalize_by_behavior(behavior_data):
    """
    Personalize content based on user behavior
    """
    if behavior_data.get('viewed_reviews', 0) > 3:
        return {
            'content_type': 'reviews_heavy',
            'elements': ['customer_reviews', 'ratings', 'testimonials']
        }
    elif behavior_data.get('viewed_comparison', False):
        return {
            'content_type': 'comparison',
            'elements': ['comparison_table', 'why_we_win', 'advantages']
        }
    elif behavior_data.get('viewed_specs', False):
        return {
            'content_type': 'technical',
            'elements': ['specifications', 'technical_details', 'expert_review']
        }
    else:
        return {
            'content_type': 'standard',
            'elements': ['benefits', 'features', 'social_proof']
        }
```

## üìä Complete Advanced Reporting 2.0

### **Custom Report Builder**

#### **Report Configuration**
```python
class CustomReportBuilder:
    def __init__(self):
        self.metrics = []
        self.dimensions = []
        self.filters = []
        self.time_range = None
    
    def add_metric(self, metric_name):
        """Add metric to report"""
        self.metrics.append(metric_name)
        return self
    
    def add_dimension(self, dimension_name):
        """Add dimension to report"""
        self.dimensions.append(dimension_name)
        return self
    
    def add_filter(self, filter_condition):
        """Add filter to report"""
        self.filters.append(filter_condition)
        return self
    
    def set_time_range(self, start_date, end_date):
        """Set time range for report"""
        self.time_range = (start_date, end_date)
        return self
    
    def build(self):
        """Build and execute report"""
        query = self.build_query()
        results = self.execute_query(query)
        return self.format_results(results)
```

### **Automated Insights**

#### **Insight Generation**
```python
def generate_insights(data):
    """
    Automatically generate insights from data
    """
    insights = []
    
    # Trend analysis
    if data['recovery_rate_trend'] == 'increasing':
        insights.append({
            'type': 'positive_trend',
            'message': f"Recovery rate increased by {data['recovery_rate_change']}%",
            'recommendation': 'Continue current strategy'
        })
    
    # Performance comparison
    if data['current_recovery_rate'] > data['industry_average']:
        insights.append({
            'type': 'above_average',
            'message': f"Recovery rate {data['current_recovery_rate']}% is above industry average",
            'recommendation': 'Maintain performance, scale successful strategies'
        })
    
    # Opportunity identification
    if data['low_performing_segment']:
        insights.append({
            'type': 'opportunity',
            'message': f"{data['low_performing_segment']} segment underperforming",
            'recommendation': f"Focus optimization efforts on {data['low_performing_segment']}"
        })
    
    return insights
```

## üé® Complete Visual Design Templates

### **Template 1: Minimalist Clean**

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Your Cart is Waiting</title>
</head>
<body style="margin: 0; padding: 0; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; background-color: #f4f4f4;">
    <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background-color: #f4f4f4;">
        <tr>
            <td align="center" style="padding: 40px 20px;">
                <table width="600" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background-color: #ffffff; border-radius: 8px;">
                    <!-- Header -->
                    <tr>
                        <td align="center" style="padding: 30px 20px;">
                            <img src="[LOGO_URL]" alt="[BRAND_NAME]" width="150" style="max-width: 150px;">
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                    <!-- Content -->
                    <tr>
                        <td style="padding: 0 40px 40px;">
                            <h1 style="margin: 0 0 20px; font-size: 28px; color: #212529;">Hi [FIRST_NAME],</h1>
                            <p style="margin: 0 0 20px; font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.6; color: #212529;">You left some items in your cart:</p>
                            
                            <!-- Product -->
                            <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="margin: 20px 0; border: 1px solid #e0e0e0; border-radius: 8px;">
                                <tr>
                                    <td style="padding: 20px;">
                                        <img src="[PRODUCT_IMAGE]" alt="[PRODUCT_NAME]" width="100" style="float: left; margin-right: 15px; border-radius: 4px;">
                                        <h3 style="margin: 0 0 10px; font-size: 20px; color: #212529;">[PRODUCT_NAME]</h3>
                                        <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: #212529;">$[PRICE] √ó [QUANTITY]</p>
                                        <div style="clear: both;"></div>
                                    </td>
                                </tr>
                            </table>
                            
                            <p style="margin: 20px 0; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: #212529;">Total: $[CART_TOTAL]</p>
                            
                            <!-- CTA -->
                            <table width="100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
                                <tr>
                                    <td align="center" style="padding: 20px 0;">
                                        <a href="[CART_URL]" style="display: inline-block; padding: 15px 40px; background-color: #007bff; color: #ffffff; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 18px;">Complete Purchase</a>
                                    </td>
                                </tr>
                            </table>
                            
                            <p style="margin: 20px 0 0; font-size: 14px; color: #6c757d;">Questions? Reply to this email.</p>
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                    <!-- Footer -->
                    <tr>
                        <td style="padding: 20px; text-align: center; font-size: 12px; color: #6c757d; border-top: 1px solid #e0e0e0;">
                            <p style="margin: 0 0 10px;">[COMPANY_NAME] | [ADDRESS]</p>

                        </td>

                </table>
            </td>

</html>
```

## üöÄ Complete Advanced Workflows 2.0

### **Workflow 5: Predictive Recovery**

```
Cart Abandoned
    ‚Üì
Calculate Recovery Probability
    ‚Üì
IF probability > 80%:
    ‚Üí Fast track (30m, 2h, 6h)
    ‚Üí Higher discount (20-25%)
    ‚Üí Premium treatment
    ‚Üí Multi-channel
ELIF probability 50-80%:
    ‚Üí Standard track (1h, 24h, 48h)
    ‚Üí Moderate discount (15-20%)
    ‚Üí Standard treatment
    ‚Üí Email + SMS
ELIF probability 30-50%:
    ‚Üí Slow track (2h, 48h, 7d)
    ‚Üí Lower discount (10-15%)
    ‚Üí Educational focus
    ‚Üí Email only
ELSE:
    ‚Üí Minimal track (48h, 7d, 14d)
    ‚Üí Minimal discount (5-10%)
    ‚Üí Value focus
    ‚Üí Email only
```

### **Workflow 6: Engagement-Based Recovery**

```
Email 1 Sent
    ‚Üì
Track Engagement (6 hours)
    ‚Üì
IF opened + clicked:
    ‚Üí Pause sequence
    ‚Üí Wait 24 hours
    ‚Üí IF purchased: Mark recovered
    ‚Üí IF not purchased: Send Email 2 (trust building)
ELIF opened but not clicked:
    ‚Üí Send Email 2 (6h later)
    ‚Üí Different angle
    ‚Üí Stronger CTA
    ‚Üí Slightly higher discount
ELIF not opened:
    ‚Üí Send Email 2 (24h later)
    ‚Üí Standard timing
    ‚Üí Different subject line
    ‚Üí Standard discount
    ‚Üì
Repeat for Email 3 and 4
```

## üìà Complete Advanced Analytics 2.0

### **Predictive Scoring Models**

#### **Recovery Probability Model**
```python
from sklearn.ensemble import GradientBoostingClassifier
import pandas as pd

def build_recovery_model(training_data):
    """
    Build model to predict recovery probability
    """
    # Features
    features = [
        'cart_value',
        'customer_segment_score',
        'time_since_abandon',
        'engagement_score',
        'product_category_score',
        'previous_purchases',
        'email_open_history',
        'email_click_history',
        'device_type',
        'location_score'
    ]
    
    X = training_data[features]
    y = training_data['recovered']  # 1 if recovered, 0 if not
    
    # Train model
    model = GradientBoostingClassifier(
        n_estimators=100,
        learning_rate=0.1,
        max_depth=5
    )
    model.fit(X, y)
    
    return model

def predict_recovery(cart_data, model):
    """
    Predict recovery probability for a cart
    """
    features = prepare_features(cart_data)
    probability = model.predict_proba([features])[0][1]
    
    return {
        'recovery_probability': probability * 100,
        'recommended_action': get_recommended_action(probability),
        'confidence': calculate_confidence(probability)
    }
```

### **Attribution Analysis**

#### **Multi-Touch Attribution**
```python
def calculate_multi_touch_attribution(conversion_path):
    """
    Calculate attribution across all touchpoints
    """
    # Time-decay model
    total_touchpoints = len(conversion_path)
    attribution = {}
    
    for i, touchpoint in enumerate(conversion_path):
        # More recent touchpoints get more credit
        weight = (i + 1) / sum(range(1, total_touchpoints + 1))
        attribution[touchpoint] = weight
    
    return attribution
```

## üéØ Complete Subject Line Generator

### **AI-Powered Generation**

#### **Generator with Templates**
```python
def generate_subject_line(cart_data, email_number, style='balanced'):
    """
    Generate subject line based on cart data and email number
    """
    templates = {
        1: {  # Reminder
            'personal': "[Name], your cart is waiting",
            'urgency': "‚è∞ Your cart expires soon, [Name]",
            'value': "Don't forget your [Product], [Name]",
            'question': "Still interested in [Product], [Name]?"
        },
        2: {  # Value
            'personal': "[Name], why [Product] is perfect for you",
            'social': "Join 10,000+ customers who love [Product]",
            'benefit': "See what you're missing, [Name]",
            'question': "Want to know why customers choose [Product]?"
        },
        3: {  # Discount
            'personal': "[Name], save [X]% on your cart",
            'urgency': "Limited time: [X]% off for [Name]",
            'value': "Special offer: Save $[Amount], [Name]",
            'exclusive': "Exclusive [X]% off just for you, [Name]"
        },
        4: {  # Final
            'urgency': "Last chance: Your cart expires in [X] hours",
            'final': "Final offer: [X]% off expires soon",
            'last': "Don't lose your discount, [Name]",
            'expiring': "Your [X]% discount expires in [X] hours"
        }
    }
    
    email_templates = templates[email_number]
    selected_template = email_templates.get(style, email_templates['personal'])
    
    # Replace placeholders
    subject = selected_template.replace('[Name]', cart_data.get('firstName', 'there'))
    subject = subject.replace('[Product]', cart_data.get('productName', 'items'))
    subject = subject.replace('[X]', str(cart_data.get('discount', 20)))
    subject = subject.replace('[Amount]', str(cart_data.get('savings', 50)))
    
    return subject
```

## üéÅ Complete Incentive Optimization Engine

### **Dynamic Incentive Calculator**

#### **Complete Calculation System**
```python
def calculate_optimal_incentive(cart_data, customer_data, market_data):
    """
    Calculate optimal incentive for maximum ROI
    """
    base_discount = 10
    
    # Cart value factor
    if cart_data['total'] > 500:
        base_discount += 8
    elif cart_data['total'] > 200:
        base_discount += 5
    elif cart_data['total'] > 100:
        base_discount += 3
    
    # Customer segment factor
    segment_multipliers = {
        'VIP': 1.5,
        'Returning': 1.2,
        'New': 1.0,
        'Price-Sensitive': 1.3
    }
    base_discount *= segment_multipliers.get(customer_data['segment'], 1.0)
    
    # Time factor
    hours = cart_data['hours_since_abandon']
    if hours > 72:
        base_discount += 5
    elif hours > 48:
        base_discount += 3
    
    # Inventory factor
    if cart_data.get('inventory_level', 100) < 10:
        base_discount += 3
    
    # Competition factor
    if market_data.get('high_competition', False):
        base_discount += 2
    
    # Cap at 30%
    final_discount = min(int(base_discount), 30)
    
    # Calculate expected ROI
    expected_recovery = predict_recovery_with_discount(cart_data, final_discount)
    expected_revenue = cart_data['total'] * (1 - final_discount/100) * expected_recovery
    discount_cost = cart_data['total'] * (final_discount/100) * expected_recovery
    expected_roi = ((expected_revenue - discount_cost) / discount_cost) * 100 if discount_cost > 0 else 0
    
    return {
        'discount': final_discount,
        'expected_recovery': expected_recovery,
        'expected_revenue': expected_revenue,
        'discount_cost': discount_cost,
        'expected_roi': expected_roi,
        'recommendation': 'proceed' if expected_roi > 300 else 'adjust'
    }
```

## üìä Complete Dashboard Implementation

### **Real-Time Monitoring Dashboard**

#### **Live Metrics Widget**
```javascript
// Real-time dashboard updates
class LiveDashboard {
    constructor() {
        this.updateInterval = 60000; // 1 minute
        this.init();
    }
    
    init() {
        this.loadMetrics();
        this.startAutoRefresh();
    }
    
    async loadMetrics() {
        const response = await fetch('/api/dashboard/metrics');
        const data = await response.json();
        
        this.updateWidgets(data);
    }
    
    updateWidgets(data) {
        // Update recovery rate
        document.getElementById('recovery-rate').textContent = 
            `${data.recovery_rate}%`;
        
        // Update revenue
        document.getElementById('revenue').textContent = 
            `$${data.revenue.toLocaleString()}`;
        
        // Update ROI
        document.getElementById('roi').textContent = 
            `${data.roi}%`;
        
        // Update charts
        this.updateCharts(data);
    }
    
    updateCharts(data) {
        // Update recovery rate chart
        this.recoveryRateChart.data.labels.push(new Date().toLocaleTimeString());
        this.recoveryRateChart.data.datasets[0].data.push(data.recovery_rate);
        this.recoveryRateChart.update();
        
        // Update revenue chart
        this.revenueChart.data.labels.push(new Date().toLocaleTimeString());
        this.revenueChart.data.datasets[0].data.push(data.revenue);
        this.revenueChart.update();
    }
    
    startAutoRefresh() {
        setInterval(() => {
            this.loadMetrics();
        }, this.updateInterval);
    }
}

// Initialize
const dashboard = new LiveDashboard();
```
