## üéØ Complete Testing Framework 2.0

### **Advanced A/B Testing**

#### **Multivariate Testing Setup**
```python
from itertools import product

def setup_multivariate_test(factors):
    """
    Set up multivariate test with multiple factors
    """
    # Example factors
    # factors = {
    #     'subject_line': ['Personal', 'Urgency', 'Value'],
    #     'discount': [15, 20, 25],
    #     'send_time': ['Morning', 'Afternoon', 'Evening']
    # }
    
    # Generate all combinations
    factor_names = list(factors.keys())
    factor_values = list(factors.values())
    combinations = list(product(*factor_values))
    
    variants = []
    for i, combo in enumerate(combinations):
        variant = dict(zip(factor_names, combo))
        variant['variant_id'] = f'variant_{i+1}'
        variants.append(variant)
    
    return variants

def analyze_multivariate_results(results):
    """
    Analyze multivariate test results
    """
    # Find best performing variant
    best_variant = max(results, key=lambda x: x['conversion_rate'])
    
    # Calculate main effects
    main_effects = calculate_main_effects(results)
    
    # Calculate interactions
    interactions = calculate_interactions(results)
    
    return {
        'best_variant': best_variant,
        'main_effects': main_effects,
        'interactions': interactions,
        'recommendations': generate_recommendations(best_variant, main_effects)
    }
```

## üöÄ Complete Automation System 3.0

### **Complete Workflow Engine**

#### **Workflow Engine Architecture**
```python
class WorkflowEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        self.workflows = {}
        self.triggers = {}
        self.actions = {}
    
    def register_workflow(self, workflow_id, workflow_config):
        """
        Register a workflow
        """
        self.workflows[workflow_id] = workflow_config
    
    def execute_workflow(self, workflow_id, context):
        """
        Execute a workflow with context
        """
        workflow = self.workflows[workflow_id]
        
        for step in workflow['steps']:
            if self.evaluate_condition(step['condition'], context):
                result = self.execute_action(step['action'], context)
                context.update(result)
                
                if step.get('stop_on_success', False) and result.get('success'):
                    break
    
    def evaluate_condition(self, condition, context):
        """
        Evaluate workflow condition
        """
        # Support for: AND, OR, NOT, comparison operators
        return eval_condition(condition, context)
    
    def execute_action(self, action, context):
        """
        Execute workflow action
        """
        action_type = action['type']
        action_config = action['config']
        
        if action_type == 'send_email':
            return self.send_email(action_config, context)
        elif action_type == 'send_sms':
            return self.send_sms(action_config, context)
        elif action_type == 'update_segment':
            return self.update_segment(action_config, context)
        elif action_type == 'wait':
            return self.wait(action_config, context)
        # ... more action types
```

### **Smart Decision Engine**

#### **Decision Tree Implementation**
```python
class DecisionTree:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = None
    
    def build_tree(self, rules):
        """
        Build decision tree from rules
        """
        self.root = self.build_node(rules)
    
    def evaluate(self, context):
        """
        Evaluate decision tree with context
        """
        return self.traverse(self.root, context)
    
    def traverse(self, node, context):
        """
        Traverse decision tree
        """
        if node.is_leaf():
            return node.action
        
        condition_result = self.evaluate_condition(node.condition, context)
        
        if condition_result:
            return self.traverse(node.true_branch, context)
        else:
            return self.traverse(node.false_branch, context)

# Example usage
rules = {
    'if': {
        'cart_value': {'>': 200},
        'customer_segment': 'VIP'
    },
    'then': {
        'sequence': 'fast_track',
        'discount': 25,
        'channels': ['email', 'sms', 'push']
    }
}
```

## üìà Complete Revenue Models

### **Revenue Projection Models**

#### **Model 1: Linear Growth**
```python
def linear_revenue_projection(current_revenue, growth_rate, periods):
    """
    Project revenue with linear growth
    """
    projections = []
    for i in range(periods):
        revenue = current_revenue * (1 + growth_rate * (i + 1))
        projections.append(revenue)
    return projections
```

#### **Model 2: Compound Growth**
```python
def compound_revenue_projection(current_revenue, growth_rate, periods):
    """
    Project revenue with compound growth
    """
    projections = []
    for i in range(periods):
        revenue = current_revenue * ((1 + growth_rate) ** (i + 1))
        projections.append(revenue)
    return projections
```

#### **Model 3: Seasonal Adjustment**
```python
def seasonal_revenue_projection(base_revenue, seasonal_factors, periods):
    """
    Project revenue with seasonal adjustments
    """
    projections = []
    for i in range(periods):
        month = (i % 12) + 1
        seasonal_factor = seasonal_factors.get(month, 1.0)
        revenue = base_revenue * seasonal_factor
        projections.append(revenue)
    return projections
```

## üéØ Complete Personalization Engine 4.0

### **Hyper-Personalization System**

#### **Complete Personalization Engine**
```python
class HyperPersonalizationEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        self.data_sources = {}
        self.personalization_rules = {}
        self.content_templates = {}
    
    def personalize_email(self, customer_id, cart_data):
        """
        Generate fully personalized email
        """
        # Gather all data
        customer_data = self.get_customer_data(customer_id)
        behavioral_data = self.get_behavioral_data(customer_id)
        contextual_data = self.get_contextual_data(customer_id)
        
        # Calculate personalization scores
        personalization_scores = self.calculate_scores(
            customer_data, behavioral_data, contextual_data
        )
        
        # Select content elements
        content_elements = self.select_content_elements(
            personalization_scores, cart_data
        )
        
        # Generate personalized content
        personalized_content = self.generate_content(
            content_elements, customer_data, cart_data
        )
        
        return personalized_content
    
    def calculate_scores(self, customer_data, behavioral_data, contextual_data):
        """
        Calculate personalization scores
        """
        return {
            'urgency_score': self.calculate_urgency(customer_data, cart_data),
            'value_score': self.calculate_value(customer_data, cart_data),
            'social_proof_score': self.calculate_social_proof(customer_data),
            'trust_score': self.calculate_trust(customer_data),
            'discount_score': self.calculate_discount_need(customer_data, cart_data)
        }
    
    def select_content_elements(self, scores, cart_data):
        """
        Select content elements based on scores
        """
        elements = []
        
        if scores['urgency_score'] > 0.7:
            elements.append('countdown_timer')
            elements.append('limited_stock')
        
        if scores['value_score'] > 0.7:
            elements.append('benefits_list')
            elements.append('use_cases')
        
        if scores['social_proof_score'] > 0.7:
            elements.append('customer_reviews')
            elements.append('testimonials')
        
        if scores['trust_score'] > 0.7:
            elements.append('trust_badges')
            elements.append('guarantees')
        
        if scores['discount_score'] > 0.7:
            elements.append('discount_offer')
            elements.append('savings_calculation')
        
        return elements
```

## üéÅ Complete Incentive Calculator

### **Interactive Calculator**

#### **JavaScript Implementation**
```javascript
class IncentiveCalculator {
    constructor() {
        this.baseDiscount = 10;
        this.factors = {
            cartValue: 0,
            customerSegment: 0,
            timeSinceAbandon: 0,
            inventoryLevel: 0,
            competition: 0
        };
    }
    
    calculate(cartValue, customerSegment, hoursSinceAbandon, inventoryLevel, highCompetition) {
        let discount = this.baseDiscount;
        
        // Cart value factor
        if (cartValue > 500) {
            discount += 8;
        } else if (cartValue > 200) {
            discount += 5;
        } else if (cartValue > 100) {
            discount += 3;
        }
        
        // Customer segment factor
        const segmentMultipliers = {
            'VIP': 1.5,
            'Returning': 1.2,
            'New': 1.0,
            'Price-Sensitive': 1.3
        };
        discount *= segmentMultipliers[customerSegment] || 1.0;
        
        // Time factor
        if (hoursSinceAbandon > 72) {
            discount += 5;
        } else if (hoursSinceAbandon > 48) {
            discount += 3;
        }
        
        // Inventory factor
        if (inventoryLevel < 10) {
            discount += 3;
        }
        
        // Competition factor
        if (highCompetition) {
            discount += 2;
        }
        
        // Cap at 30%
        discount = Math.min(Math.round(discount), 30);
        
        // Calculate expected results
        const savings = cartValue * (discount / 100);
        const finalPrice = cartValue - savings;
        
        return {
            discount: discount,
            savings: savings,
            finalPrice: finalPrice,
            originalPrice: cartValue
        };
    }
}

// Usage
const calculator = new IncentiveCalculator();
const result = calculator.calculate(200, 'Returning', 48, 5, false);
console.log(`Recommended discount: ${result.discount}%`);
console.log(`Customer saves: $${result.savings}`);
console.log(`Final price: $${result.finalPrice}`);
```

## üìä Complete Reporting System 2.0

### **Automated Report Generation**

#### **Report Scheduler**
```python
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import schedule
import time

def generate_daily_report():
    """
    Generate daily performance report
    """
    yesterday = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)
    
    report = {
        'date': yesterday.strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),
        'metrics': {
            'emails_sent': get_emails_sent(yesterday),
            'emails_opened': get_emails_opened(yesterday),
            'emails_clicked': get_emails_clicked(yesterday),
            'recoveries': get_recoveries(yesterday),
            'revenue': get_revenue(yesterday),
            'recovery_rate': calculate_recovery_rate(yesterday),
            'roi': calculate_roi(yesterday)
        },
        'insights': generate_insights(yesterday),
        'recommendations': generate_recommendations(yesterday)
    }
    
    # Send report
    send_report(report, recipients=['team@example.com'])
    
    return report

def generate_weekly_report():
    """
    Generate weekly performance report
    """
    week_start = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=7)
    
    report = {
        'period': f"{week_start.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} to {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}",
        'summary': generate_weekly_summary(week_start),
        'trends': analyze_trends(week_start),
        'top_performers': get_top_performers(week_start),
        'improvements': get_improvements(week_start)
    }
    
    send_report(report, recipients=['team@example.com', 'management@example.com'])
    
    return report

# Schedule reports
schedule.every().day.at("09:00").do(generate_daily_report)
schedule.every().monday.at("09:00").do(generate_weekly_report)

# Run scheduler
while True:
    schedule.run_pending()
    time.sleep(60)
```

const eventSchema = {
    // Event identification
    event_id: 'string (UUID)',
    event_type: 'string (cart_abandoned, email_sent, email_opened, etc.)',
    timestamp: 'datetime (ISO 8601)',

    customer_segment: 'string',

    cart_items: 'array',
    item_count: 'number',

    email_number: 'number (1-4)',
    email_type: 'string (reminder, value, discount, final)',
    subject_line: 'string',
    
    // Engagement data
    opened: 'boolean',
    clicked: 'boolean',
    converted: 'boolean',
    opened_at: 'datetime',
    clicked_at: 'datetime',
    converted_at: 'datetime',
    
    // Contextual data
    device_type: 'string (desktop, mobile, tablet)',
    browser: 'string',
    location: 'object (country, city, timezone)',
    referrer: 'string',
    
    // Performance data
    recovery_channel: 'string (email, sms, push, etc.)',
    discount_used: 'number',
    revenue: 'number',
    
    // Metadata
    session_id: 'string',
    user_agent: 'string',
    ip_address: 'string (hashed)'
};

ELSE:
    ‚Üí Standard sequence

## üìà Complete Forecasting System 2.0

### **Advanced Prediction Models**

#### **Model 6: Time Series Forecasting**
```python
from statsmodels.tsa.arima.model import ARIMA
import pandas as pd

def time_series_forecast(historical_data, periods=30):
    """
    Forecast using ARIMA time series model
    """
    # Prepare data
    ts_data = pd.Series(historical_data['recovery_rate'], 
                       index=pd.date_range(start='2024-01-01', 
                                          periods=len(historical_data),
                                          freq='D'))
    
    # Fit ARIMA model
    model = ARIMA(ts_data, order=(1, 1, 1))
    fitted_model = model.fit()
    
    # Forecast
    forecast = fitted_model.forecast(steps=periods)
    confidence_intervals = fitted_model.get_forecast(steps=periods).conf_int()
    
    return {
        'forecast': forecast.tolist(),
        'confidence_intervals': confidence_intervals.values.tolist(),
        'model_summary': fitted_model.summary()
    }
```

#### **Model 7: Ensemble Forecasting**
```python
def ensemble_forecast_v2(historical_data, periods=30):
    """
    Advanced ensemble forecasting combining multiple models
    """
    # Model 1: Linear regression
    linear_forecast = linear_regression_forecast(historical_data, periods)
    
    # Model 2: ARIMA
    arima_forecast = time_series_forecast(historical_data, periods)
    
    # Model 3: ML model
    ml_forecast = ml_revenue_forecast(historical_data, periods)
    
    # Model 4: Seasonal decomposition
    seasonal_forecast = seasonal_decomposition_forecast(historical_data, periods)
    
    # Weighted ensemble (ML gets most weight)
    weights = [0.15, 0.20, 0.45, 0.20]
    ensemble_forecast = (
        linear_forecast * weights[0] +
        arima_forecast * weights[1] +
        ml_forecast * weights[2] +
        seasonal_forecast * weights[3]
    )
    
    return {
        'ensemble_forecast': ensemble_forecast,
        'individual_forecasts': {
            'linear': linear_forecast,
            'arima': arima_forecast,
            'ml': ml_forecast,
            'seasonal': seasonal_forecast
        },
        'weights': weights
    }
```

## üéØ Complete Advanced Targeting 2.0

### **Lookalike Audience Creation**

#### **Python Implementation**
```python
from sklearn.neighbors import NearestNeighbors
import pandas as pd

def create_lookalike_audience(high_value_customers, all_customers, n_neighbors=1000):
    """
    Create lookalike audience based on high-value customers
    """
    # Features for matching
    features = [
        'age', 'gender', 'location_score', 'device_type',
        'browsing_behavior', 'purchase_history_score',
        'engagement_score', 'product_preferences'
    ]
    
    # Prepare data
    high_value_features = high_value_customers[features]
    all_features = all_customers[features]
    
    # Fit nearest neighbors
    nn = NearestNeighbors(n_neighbors=n_neighbors, metric='cosine')
    nn.fit(high_value_features)
    
    # Find lookalikes
    distances, indices = nn.kneighbors(all_features)
    
    # Create lookalike audience
    lookalike_audience = all_customers.iloc[indices.flatten()].drop_duplicates()
    
    return {
        'lookalike_audience': lookalike_audience,
        'similarity_scores': 1 - distances.flatten(),
        'audience_size': len(lookalike_audience)
    }
```

### **Retargeting List Optimization**

#### **List Segmentation**
```python
def optimize_retargeting_lists(customers):
    """
    Optimize retargeting lists for maximum ROI
    """
    lists = {
        'high_intent': [],
        'medium_intent': [],
        'low_intent': [],
        'price_sensitive': [],
        'research_focused': []
    }
    
    for customer in customers:
        intent_score = calculate_intent_score(customer)
        price_sensitivity = calculate_price_sensitivity(customer)
        research_level = calculate_research_level(customer)
        
        if intent_score > 0.8:
            lists['high_intent'].append(customer)
        elif intent_score > 0.5:
            lists['medium_intent'].append(customer)
        else:
            lists['low_intent'].append(customer)
        
        if price_sensitivity > 0.7:
            lists['price_sensitive'].append(customer)
        
        if research_level > 0.7:
            lists['research_focused'].append(customer)
    
    return lists
```

## üõ†Ô∏è Complete Technical Implementation 3.0

### **Complete Backend API**

#### **Flask API Implementation**
```python
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from flask_cors import CORS
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import json

app = Flask(__name__)
CORS(app)

class CartRecoveryAPI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.db = self.init_database()
    
    @app.route('/api/cart/track', methods=['POST'])
    def track_cart(self):
        """
        Track cart update
        """
        data = request.json
        
        cart = {
            'cart_id': data.get('cart_id'),
            'customer_email': data.get('email'),
            'customer_first_name': data.get('firstName'),
            'cart_items': json.dumps(data.get('items', [])),
            'cart_total': data.get('total', 0),
            'updated_at': datetime.now()
        }
        
        # Save to database
        cart_id = self.save_cart(cart)
        
        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'cart_id': cart_id
        })
    
    @app.route('/api/cart/abandon', methods=['POST'])
    def track_abandonment(self):
        """
        Track cart abandonment
        """
        data = request.json
        
        abandonment = {
            'cart_id': data.get('cart_id'),
            'customer_email': data.get('email'),
            'abandoned_at': datetime.now(),
            'cart_value': data.get('total', 0)
        }
        
        # Save abandonment
        abandonment_id = self.save_abandonment(abandonment)
        
        # Trigger recovery sequence
        self.trigger_recovery_sequence(abandonment)
        
        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'abandonment_id': abandonment_id
        })
    
    @app.route('/api/cart/recover', methods=['POST'])
    def track_recovery(self):
        """
        Track cart recovery
        """
        data = request.json
        
        recovery = {
            'cart_id': data.get('cart_id'),
            'customer_email': data.get('email'),
            'recovered_at': datetime.now(),
            'revenue': data.get('revenue', 0),
            'email_number': data.get('email_number'),
            'discount_used': data.get('discount', 0)
        }
        
        # Save recovery
        recovery_id = self.save_recovery(recovery)
        
        # Update analytics
        self.update_analytics(recovery)
        
        return jsonify({
            'success': True,
            'recovery_id': recovery_id
        })
    
    @app.route('/api/analytics/dashboard', methods=['GET'])
    def get_dashboard_data(self):
        """
        Get dashboard data
        """
        period = request.args.get('period', '30d')
        
        data = {
            'recovery_rate': self.calculate_recovery_rate(period),
            'revenue_recovered': self.calculate_revenue(period),
            'roi': self.calculate_roi(period),
            'email_performance': self.get_email_performance(period),
            'segment_performance': self.get_segment_performance(period)
        }
        
        return jsonify(data)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    api = CartRecoveryAPI()
    app.run(debug=True, port=5000)
```

## üéÅ Complete Incentive Strategy 3.0

### **Advanced Incentive Combinations**

#### **Combination 1: Discount + Free Shipping**
```
Strategy: Combine percentage discount with free shipping
Best For: Medium to high value carts
Message: "Save [X]% + Free Shipping"
Value: High perceived value
Cost: Moderate
```

#### **Combination 2: Discount + Free Gift**
```
Strategy: Combine discount with free gift
Best For: High value carts
Message: "Save [X]% + Free [Gift] (Value: $[Amount])"
Value: Very high perceived value
Cost: Higher
```

#### **Combination 3: Free Shipping + Free Gift**
```
Strategy: Non-discount incentives
Best For: Premium brands
Message: "Free Shipping + Free [Gift]"
Value: High perceived value
Cost: Lower (no discount)
```

#### **Combination 4: Discount + Early Access**
```
Strategy: Combine discount with exclusivity
Best For: New product launches
Message: "Save [X]% + Early Access to [Product]"
Value: High perceived value
Cost: Moderate
```

#### **Combination 5: Maximum Value Package**
```
Strategy: All incentives combined
Best For: Very high value carts
Message: "Save [X]% + Free Shipping + Free [Gift] + Early Access"
Value: Maximum perceived value
Cost: Highest
```

## üìä Complete Analytics Dashboard 3.0

### **Real-Time Monitoring System**

#### **Live Dashboard Implementation**
```javascript
// Complete real-time dashboard
class RealTimeDashboard {
    constructor() {
        this.metrics = {};
        this.charts = {};
        this.updateInterval = 30000; // 30 seconds
        this.init();
    }
    
    init() {
        this.setupCharts();
        this.startUpdates();
        this.setupAlerts();
    }
    
    setupCharts() {
        // Recovery rate chart
        this.recoveryRateChart = new Chart(document.getElementById('recovery-rate-chart'), {
            type: 'line',
            data: {
                labels: [],
                datasets: [{
                    label: 'Recovery Rate',
                    data: [],
                    borderColor: '#007bff',
                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(0, 123, 255, 0.1)'
                }]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true,
                scales: {
                    y: {
                        beginAtZero: true,
                        max: 100
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        
        // Revenue chart
        this.revenueChart = new Chart(document.getElementById('revenue-chart'), {
            type: 'bar',
            data: {
                labels: [],
                datasets: [{
                    label: 'Revenue Recovered',
                    data: [],
                    backgroundColor: '#28a745'
                }]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true
            }
        });
    }
    
    async updateMetrics() {
        const response = await fetch('/api/dashboard/metrics');
        const data = await response.json();
        
        // Update metrics
        this.updateMetricWidget('recovery-rate', data.recovery_rate, '%');
        this.updateMetricWidget('revenue', data.revenue, '$');
        this.updateMetricWidget('roi', data.roi, '%');
        
        // Update charts
        this.updateCharts(data);
        
        // Check alerts
        this.checkAlerts(data);
    }
    
    updateMetricWidget(id, value, unit) {
        const element = document.getElementById(id);
        if (element) {
            const formattedValue = typeof value === 'number' 
                ? value.toLocaleString() 
                : value;
            element.textContent = `${formattedValue}${unit}`;
        }
    }
    
    updateCharts(data) {
        const now = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
        
        // Update recovery rate chart
        this.recoveryRateChart.data.labels.push(now);
        this.recoveryRateChart.data.datasets[0].data.push(data.recovery_rate);
        
        // Keep only last 20 data points
        if (this.recoveryRateChart.data.labels.length > 20) {
            this.recoveryRateChart.data.labels.shift();
            this.recoveryRateChart.data.datasets[0].data.shift();
        }
        
        this.recoveryRateChart.update('none');
        
        // Update revenue chart
        this.revenueChart.data.labels.push(now);
        this.revenueChart.data.datasets[0].data.push(data.revenue);
        
        if (this.revenueChart.data.labels.length > 20) {
            this.revenueChart.data.labels.shift();
            this.revenueChart.data.datasets[0].data.shift();
        }
        
        this.revenueChart.update('none');
    }
    
    setupAlerts() {
        this.alerts = {
            'recovery_rate_low': { threshold: 15, triggered: false },
            'revenue_drop': { threshold: -10, triggered: false }
        };
    }
    
    checkAlerts(data) {
        // Check recovery rate
        if (data.recovery_rate < this.alerts.recovery_rate_low.threshold) {
            if (!this.alerts.recovery_rate_low.triggered) {
                this.showAlert('Recovery rate is below target!', 'warning');
                this.alerts.recovery_rate_low.triggered = true;
            }
        }
        
        // Check revenue drop
        const revenueChange = this.calculateRevenueChange(data.revenue);
        if (revenueChange < this.alerts.revenue_drop.threshold) {
            if (!this.alerts.revenue_drop.triggered) {
                this.showAlert('Revenue dropped significantly!', 'error');
                this.alerts.revenue_drop.triggered = true;
            }
        }
    }
    
    showAlert(message, type) {
        // Show alert notification
        console.log(`[${type.toUpperCase()}] ${message}`);
        // Implement actual alert UI
    }
    
    startUpdates() {
        // Initial load
        this.updateMetrics();
        
        // Set up interval
        setInterval(() => {
            this.updateMetrics();
        }, this.updateInterval);
    }
}

// Initialize
const dashboard = new RealTimeDashboard();
```

## üéØ Complete Optimization Playbook 2.0

### **Optimization by Problem**

#### **Problem 1: Low Open Rates**
```
Diagnosis:
- Check subject lines
- Review send times
- Analyze list quality
- Check deliverability

Solutions:
1. A/B test subject lines
2. Optimize send times
3. Clean email list
4. Improve deliverability
5. Add personalization

Expected Improvement: +5-10% open rate
```

#### **Problem 2: Low Click Rates**
```
Diagnosis:
- Review email content
- Check CTA placement
- Analyze design
- Test mobile experience

Solutions:
1. Improve CTAs
2. Enhance content
3. Fix design issues
4. Optimize mobile
5. Add value proposition

Expected Improvement: +2-5% click rate
```

#### **Problem 3: Low Conversion Rates**
```
Diagnosis:
- Review offers
- Check checkout process
- Analyze trust elements
- Test discount levels

Solutions:
1. Improve offers
2. Fix checkout
3. Build trust
4. Test discounts
5. Add guarantees

Expected Improvement: +3-7% conversion rate
```

#### **Problem 4: High Unsubscribe Rate**
```
Diagnosis:
- Check email frequency
- Review content relevance
- Analyze segmentation
- Test messaging

Solutions:
1. Reduce frequency
2. Improve relevance
3. Better segmentation
4. Refine messaging
5. Add preferences

Expected Improvement: -50% unsubscribe rate
```
